The lifespan of the British people today is higher than that of their ancestors, so it is their responsibility to make their increased years worth living. If men and women want to live worthwhile lives, they must make their minds and bodies healthy. The government believes that physical education and development must occupy a fixed and special position in the national health system. Current Affairs Commentary

On Eden's Foreign Policy Speech

— Hua

The British Foreign Secretary Eden's foreign policy speech in Parliament on the 5th of this month can occupy an important page in Eden's personal political history and in the entire diplomatic history of the British Empire. His beautiful rhetoric, profound implications, broad hints, firm stance are different from the timid Simon, and different from the exaggerated and stubborn Hoare. Today, when the international aggression front is actively threatening the peace front, this young foreign minister can be said to have expressed a clear indication of British diplomacy, which has been hesitant and hesitant. That was a response to Hitler's Nuremberg speech, and also a response to Mussolini's Milan speech. In today's increasingly acute struggle between the two major international fronts, we cannot but believe that such a clear indication is of epoch-making importance.

Upholding the League of Nations and the collective security system, maintaining close friendly relations with France and Belgium, and maintaining friendly relations with Germany, but not implying exclusion or opposition to other countries. Expressing regret for the misunderstanding of Italy, but believing that the UK's transportation routes in the Mediterranean must be guaranteed. In addition, hoping for a peaceful resolution of the Sino-Japanese relationship in the Far East. These are the main contents of Eden's speech. These contents show the UK's clear attitude in the current international situation, that is, he leans towards the peace front, and issues a fairly tough warning to the aggression front. Perhaps the only "fly in the ointment" is Eden's view of the situation in the Far East. It is right for the UK to hope for peace in the Far East, but he said that the current Sino-Japanese situation has seen significant easing, which is inevitably using subjective hope to cover up the development of the objective situation. However, in any case, it is a fact that the UK is gradually and firmly shifting from an ambiguous speculative attitude to the peace front. And this fact is gratifying. Therefore, we should base on Eden's speech to briefly discuss the impact of the future diplomatic trends of the UK on the world situation, especially the situation in the two dangerous centers of Europe and the Far East.

Here, we must first mention the role of the UK in the international struggles in Europe and the Far East. Simply put, in the struggle between the two major groups of Germany and France or France and Italy in Europe, the UK stands in a pivotal position. In the Far East, in the opposition between Japan and the United States or Japan and the Soviet Union, the situation is the same. This pivotal leverage played a role in the past stage in the UK's struggle to win and maintain world hegemony. This advantageous position has also sown the seeds of speculation among the conservatives in power, resulting in adverse consequences for international development. For example, Japan's invasion of the Asian continent, the advancement of Germany's military ambitions under Hitler's rule, and the UK's speculative indulgence are all inextricably linked. However, the rise of several aggressive forces in the world has finally hit the vested interests of even those who engage in speculation and opportunism. What is especially important is that these aggressors want to rapidly plunge the whole world into war in order to realize their dream of redistributing the world. What the UK needs in the end is to maintain the status quo and conserve peace. In this way, with the increasing approach of new wars in the world and the very clear division of the two major international fronts, the UK can no longer play his old trick of speculation, and must choose a definite position in the two major fronts of aggression and peace.

Italy's annexation of Abyssinia, the completion of Germany's huge armaments, and the fascist forces' intervention in Spain are the main driving forces that forced the UK to make a decision immediately in the rapidly developing European situation. Now the UK has clearly expressed its friendship with France and believes that the contradictions between Italy and Italy in the Mediterranean are irreconcilable. As for Germany, despite singing the tune of anti-Soviet Union in the Nuremberg Congress, despite the fact that the first document that Ribbentrop took out of his briefcase after arriving in London was a common anti-Soviet Union, the cold response that Eden is now giving is not to oppose other countries. Obviously, the UK now has deeper trust in the Soviet Union's peaceful policy. Since the conclusion of the Anglo-Soviet naval agreement, this trust has been increasing. Even Churchill, the most stubborn conservative, now has to say that a peaceful Soviet Union is an indispensable factor in maintaining the balance of power in East Asia.

However, the UK's current view of Europe and the Far East is certainly a bit different. What he is most concerned about should be Europe, which is close at hand. As a result, Foreign Secretary Eden's assessment of the current situation in the Far East inevitably covers up the actual development of the serious situation with subjective demands and hopes for temporary peace. However, sooner or later, the UK will not be able to maintain this view of the development of the situation in the Pacific. He especially needs to understand that it is impossible to promote compromise in the Far East solely based on his subjective hope. The only possible way is to combine several major peaceful forces in the Pacific and jointly resist the aggressors. The United States, the Soviet Union, Britain, and China can all participate in this combination. Any country without aggressive ambitions can participate.

We cannot say that the UK has no such awareness. The recent conclusion of the Anglo-American-French currency agreement, the general diplomatic rapprochement between Britain and the United States, and the UK's recognition of the Soviet Union's naval needs in the Pacific in the Anglo-Soviet naval agreement can all be seen as signs of this trend. Naturally, we should also make greater efforts to promote the realization of this collective peace alliance in the Pacific.

Roosevelt Plans to Convene, International Peace Conference, Decides to Attend in Person, Opening Ceremony of the Americas Conference

(Washington) Well-informed sources recently stated that President Roosevelt is now preparing to convene an international conference to discuss ways to maintain peace. If this conference can be convened in the United States, he intends to attend in person. In addition, the Americas Peace Conference is scheduled to be held on December 1 in the capital of Argentina, which is particularly valued by the President, because he wants to use the cooperative approach of the Americas countries to satirize Europe, so that they know what to emulate. (Havas, 6th)

The President is scheduled to stay in the capital of Brazil for one day on November 26. Before Mr. Gibson announced this matter, President Roosevelt told reporters that he very much hoped to attend the Americas Peace Conference, but he could not make any concrete decisions before next week. New Japanese Parliament Building, Inauguration Ceremony Held Yesterday, More Than 3,800 Attended, British Ambassador Considered it the First in the World

(Tokyo) The inauguration ceremony of the new Diet Building was held on the morning of the 7th in the large open space in front of the main gate. About 3,800 dignitaries from the military, political, business, education, and construction sectors, as well as all members of the old and new Houses of Parliament, attended. At 11 o'clock, fireworks were set off as a signal, and all members stood up and played the music of Kimigayo. Thirty-four years ago, when I was a third-class secretary serving at the embassy, there was a foreigners' tennis club in a corner of Nagatacho. I was the secretary of the club and practiced tennis there all the time. Now it has been rebuilt into a magnificent Diet Building, which is indeed the first in the world. It is also surprising to hear that the building materials are all domestic. The British Parliament was built a hundred years ago, and it was the most modern at the time, but it is far from being comparable now." (Domei, 7th) As a result of the consultation of the top leadership with the Army Minister as the center, it was decided to aim at the conclusion of the deliberation of the five-minister conference as the immediate goal, and to pay close attention to the time and result of its conclusion. However, if the result of the five-minister conference is too contrary to the original purpose of the military, the army will once again open its own opinions and, in view of the internal and external situations, will have to move forward towards what it believes. Therefore, regarding the issue of renovating the parliament, depending on the outcome of the five-minister conference, there is a risk of further aggravation. (Domei, 7th)

US Finance, Striving to Balance the Budget

(Washington) Senior government officials indicated today that the government's future fiscal plan intends to find ways to balance the next budget. The government's fiscal policy is as follows: (1) Current expenditures for the next year will be reduced by $140,000,000 from $1,257,000,000; (2) Maintain current taxes; (3) Reduce new borrowing; (4) Continue to collect surplus taxes; (5) The Sino-American silver purchase agreement is about to expire and will not be continued; (6) Continue the domestic silver purchase policy; (7) Continue the world monetary stability policy; (8) Maintain the equalization fund; (9) The President continues to have the power to change the gold price of the dollar; (10) Reduce the gold reserves of the three-nation currency agreement, thereby reducing excess reserves and promoting domestic financial stability. Treasury officials said the government will implement a pay-as-you-go policy and reduce the national debt in two years. However, the known expenditures for this year have already exceeded the Treasury's revenue. Before the government reduces the national debt, the national debt may reach $35,000,000,000. The Treasury expects tax revenue for this year to reach $60,000,000,000. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt met with reporters today and hinted that the government may ask Congress to extend the period for reducing the yuan's price in order to cope with the international monetary situation. The US reduction of currency value will expire on January 30 next year. According to the bill previously passed by Congress, the gold content of the dollar has been reduced to 59.06 percent, and if necessary, it will still be reduced to 50 percent. Expiring at the same time as this dollar devaluation on January 30 next year is a $200 million equalization fund. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated that this fund is very beneficial to world currency stability, so he will propose to maintain it. (National Telegram, 6th)

(Note) The new Japanese Diet Building is 720 feet wide and 360 feet deep. The House of Peers is on the right end, with 460 seats. The House of Representatives is on the left end, with 466 seats. The total construction cost is 25 million yuan, and it took 17 years to complete.

National Trade is Weak, Japan's Imports Exceeds Exports by Nine Times Compared to Last Year, Britain and the United States also Have Import Surpluses, Germany Alone Has an Export Surplus

(Tokyo) In the first half of this year, Japan's trade balance saw a sharp increase in imports. The second half of the year should have been a period of export surpluses, but exports were unexpectedly weak, making the future very pessimistic. Comparing with the three countries of Britain, the United States, and Germany, only Germany has a better export surplus. Britain and the United States are the same as Japan, suffering from huge import surpluses. According to a survey by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, from January to the end of September this year, the trade volume of the four countries of Britain, the United States, Japan, and Germany showed that Germany's import surplus was more than 300,000 marks in the same period last year, but this year it has turned into a large export surplus of 319 million marks. On the other hand, the United States' export surplus in the same period last year was 66 million, but this year it has turned into an import surplus of 33 million. Britain and Japan are the same as last year, still having import surpluses, and the amount is even greater than last year. Britain's import surplus increased by 32% compared to last year, while Japan's reached 900% (nine times). Since the beginning of this year, due to the dangerous international situation and the volatility of the international exchange market, these negative factors have been actually reflected. The advancement of Germany, which is determined to revive, in the international trade war is truly remarkable. (Domei News Agency, 7th)

Jehol Under Poisoning: Puppet Authorities Corrupting Public Morality, Bestowing Petty Favors on the Ignorant Masses, Searching and Torturing Intellectuals

Northern Ping Communication: Recently, Mr. Li, whose ancestral home is Jehol, said that his father, Mr. Someone, once served as a member of the first National Assembly. Since the capital moved south, he has retired to his garden. When Jehol fell, he was unable to escape because he was in his hometown, so he witnessed all the measures taken in Jehol after its occupation. Mr. Li described the situation in great detail, which is abridged below to show a glimpse of the situation in Jehol:

The Someone party in Jehol is vigorously promoting the planting of opium and forcing farmers to plant it. After the harvest, the Someone party collects and buys as much as possible, using heavy trucks to transport it to Tianjin, Ping, and other places, specifically for the manufacture of morphine and other narcotics. The purpose of forcing the people to promote the planting of opium is not only to collect more opium taxes to finance military needs, but also to manufacture narcotics to induce people to consume them, directly weakening our race. This is the viciousness of their poisoning and anesthetizing policy, which is truly frightening.

The Someone party has also established many entertainment venues in Jehol, hiring Chinese traitors through vagrants to rent houses and set up venues. These venues include prostitutes (mostly Someone country prostitutes, occasionally mixed with Korean or Chinese prostitutes), gambling (such as mahjong, pai gow, playing cards, betting, and other gambling tools, all available), narcotics (such as opium, morphine, heroin), and alcoholic beverages (all kinds of alcoholic beverages are available). In addition, there are also musical plays (such as Erhuang, Bangzi Opera, Lihua Dagushu, Su Tan, Huai Diao, and other ditties). In short, everything that can induce and anesthetize the people is available, and the prices are extremely low. It only costs two jiao to enter the venue and buy a venue ticket. After entering the venue, the first thing to do is to draw a lottery. If you win the first prize, you can get something worth dozens of yuan. If you don't win, you can still use the original ticket to buy things, smoke, drink, gamble, watch plays, or watch prostitutes. Therefore, young people, ignorant masses, and frivolous women are all seduced by their deception. Vagrants and Chinese traitors can not only make huge profits by opening these entertainment venues, but also induce the Chinese people to fall, and their plans are also extremely vicious. This is more harmful to the national economy and corrupting of national morality than forcing the people to plant opium.

The puppet authorities are also trying to win the favor of the common people by drastically cutting various agencies. In each county, in addition to the county government, public security bureau, prison, and detention center, all other agencies, such as education and construction, have been reduced or eliminated. Therefore, the local taxes added to the land tax in each county have been greatly reduced, and the burden on the people has been superficially lightened. The general ignorant masses are also deceived by them and quite a few sing praises of their political achievements. Who knows that in fact they are implementing a policy of deceiving the people, so they have stopped or reduced important policies such as education and construction, adopting a passive attitude in everything in order to gradually reduce the people's knowledge, skills, and level, so that they can be easily ruled. Therefore, their surface pretext is to reduce harsh taxes to relieve the people's plight, but in reality, it is a policy of deceiving the people.

The puppet authorities are extremely thorough in handling police affairs and checking household registrations, especially for the intellectual class, such as teachers, students, or former civil servants. They investigate their family circumstances and relationships with relatives and friends in detail. Their intention is to guard against these intellectuals. If they are deemed to have suspicious behavior, they will be arrested and taken to the police station for brutal interrogation, often dying under the cane. Those who are fortunate enough to survive are often disabled or demented due to excessive torture. Therefore, they are more lenient towards ignorant and illiterate people, but extremely cruel and tyrannical towards intellectuals.

Also, their method of preventing popular unrest is to collect firearms. When the Japanese army first arrived in Jehol, they immediately issued an order requiring all people who had firearms and ammunition in their possession to register them within a certain period of time. Not long after registration, they issued another order requiring all firearms to be handed over to the puppet authorities and not allowed to be privately hidden among the people. The puppet authorities would issue a price. Initially, the puppet authorities issued 30 yuan for each gun. Later, they raised the price to 50 yuan. Now, they issue 120 yuan for each gun. The price of guns in the local folk market has always been no more than 50 or 60 yuan. Now, the puppet authorities are buying them, which is more than 100 yuan higher than the normal price. Therefore, the guns in the folk market have been almost completely searched and none remain. Their method of preventing the people can also be said to be meticulous.

Snake Zone Discovered in Northern Manchuria, Located in Keshan and the Wudalianchi Lake Area, Snake Population More Numerous Than Kyushu and Taiwan Combined

Harbin Correspondence: The Japanese in our Northeast send people to conduct investigations at any time and place. According to Japanese propaganda, Kyushu and Taiwan have always been snake-producing areas because they are both tropical regions and their archipelagoes and sandy reefs are extremely suitable for snakes to live in, so they are called natural snake-producing areas. However, it has never been seen that a snake-producing area has been discovered in northern Manchuria, which is extremely cold at minus 30 degrees Celsius, and that its output is more than that of Kyushu and Taiwan. The snake-producing area was discovered by a Japanese zoologist named Ichiro Fukushima. The locations are Keshan in Kedong County and the hot spring area near Wudalianchi Lake in the northeast of Dedu County. The climate in these two places is extremely cold, but snakes can survive there because there are many rocks near the volcanic area. Although the climate is severely cold to minus 30 degrees Celsius, the snakes live in the rocks (because the rocks have a natural lava body, which is extremely warm) and are at their most rampant. They often wrap around people in their sleep, and the clothes they wear are unknowingly inhabited by snakes. Therefore, Keshan is called Snake Mountain. The area near Wudalianchi Lake produces the most snakes. The fifteen kilometers around the lake are all rocky, and many snakes and insects live here. It has now become a snake's nest.

Obstacles to Anti-Smuggling in North China: Japanese Side Expresses Concerns to the Hebei-Chahar Authorities, Road Transport Inspection Office Moves to Tianjin with No Progress, Cangyan Coastal Defense Inspection Office Secretly Sells Verification Forms

Tianjin Correspondence: The General Inspection Office for Road Transport Anti-Smuggling of the Ministry of Finance moved to Tianjin on November 2, located at No. 1 Wu Ma Road in the Italian Concession. Deputy Director Li Tonghua instructed all staff to start working on the 3rd. Deputy Director Li Pengshou also arrived in Tianjin on the 5th to assist with everything. Director General An Si'er was originally scheduled to come to Tianjin on the 8th to preside over the office, but after receiving Li Tonghua's report, he temporarily stayed in Beijing to discuss with the Ministry of Finance. He will only come north after concrete measures are obtained. After the office moved to Tianjin, the internal organization remained the same. The original intention was to set up one or two branch offices in the important areas of the Ping-Sui Railway and the Ping-Jin section of the Bei-Ning Railway to intercept smuggled goods from being transported out of Tianjin. Li Tonghua visited Sun Weidong, Superintendent of the Tianjin Customs, and Mei Weiliang, Tianjin Customs Commissioner, several times to exchange opinions on intercepting smuggling and also visited the municipal authorities and the Public Security Bureau to request assistance. In terms of authority, it is also planned to clearly divide responsibilities with the Tianjin Customs. The Customs is responsible for intercepting smuggling on the suburban land and water traffic routes, while the Road Transport Inspection Office specializes in intercepting smuggling on the railway lines. However, while the regulations are clear, difficulties arise in implementation. It is said that certain country smugglers, fearing that the Road Transport Inspection Office's move would lead to anti-smuggling measures, fabricated rumors.

The rumor said that the mission of the Inspection Office was to support the development of British and American commercial power in North China and deliberately suppress the free entry and exit of Japanese merchants. The Japanese military and the Japanese Consulate General were misled by this floating rumor and feared that the Inspection Office would actually have this effect. Once British and American commercial power develops in North China, conflicts will inevitably arise, so they expressed to the Hebei-Chahar authorities that if they seriously assist the Inspection Office in anti-smuggling and unexpected disputes arise as a result, the Chinese side must be responsible. Under the threat, the Hebei-Chahar authorities did not dare to publicly assist the Inspection Office. As a result of Li Tonghua's visits to various authorities in Tianjin, they all believed that if diplomatic channels were not opened, taking strict anti-smuggling measures would cause trouble. Li looked around and found that the only one standing on the same front as the office was the Tianjin Customs. However, the Customs is in the same difficult situation. Although the office has opened, it has not yet performed its duties. Therefore, Li Tonghua returned to Beijing to ask for instructions, hoping to obtain clear instructions from the central government before returning to Tianjin to work.

In the past month, the amount of smuggled goods smuggled out of Tianjin Customs was countless. Although the cards intercepted some, the amount was not much. On November 5, Datong Company, a certain country smuggling merchant at No. 20 Yamaguchi Street, Japanese Concession, transported 184 bolts of cotton cloth (60 pieces per bolt) from Dalian. After the Jidong pseudo-Beidaihe Inspection Office collected taxes and issued tax bills, it was transported to Tianjin. Between the Tianjin East Station and the International Bridge, it was intercepted by Customs officers and immediately detained. The total value of the goods was more than 90,000 yuan. The smuggling merchant immediately reported to the Japanese Consulate. Consul General Horiuchi then sent Deputy Consul Yongai Xunyi to the Customs to negotiate and demand the return of the goods. The Customs refused. In the afternoon, the Japanese Consulate sent another protest letter, pointing out that the goods had already been taxed in Jidong and should be recognized as legitimate imports and cannot be detained or confiscated. The wording was very strong. The Customs has not yet responded. This is likely to be a return to the rampant smuggling situation of the spring. The Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office was ordered to close at the end of June, but the person in charge was still unwilling to give up. Recently, he secretly restored the Cangyan Coastal Defense Inspection Office and set up an office at No. 2 Ma Road in Special Zone 2. Although it has not been approved by the Hebei-Chahar authorities to collect taxes, many of the smuggled goods transported out of Tianjin in recent days have affixed with the office's verification certificate. In fact, the office has probably secretly sold vouchers for the release of smuggled goods. (6th)

Representatives of the Tobacco Industry in Guangdong Province Hosted the Press Yesterday

The two tobacco and tobacco leaf associations of Guangdong Province, as well as the farmers, elected representatives Wu Yuqiang, Su Dingchuan, Lu Yinong, and Fang Yuwan, a total of four people, to go to Beijing to petition, requesting the abolition of the monopoly on local tobacco. The representatives arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and have been preparing written justifications in recent days, separately requesting assistance from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Guangdong Association of Shanghai Compatriots, and other relevant organizations. At noon yesterday, they also hosted reporters from various newspapers in this city at the YMCA, stating various obstructive circumstances, and decided to go to Beijing tomorrow (Monday) to separately submit petitions to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government, requesting the abolition of the monopoly in order to alleviate the people's difficulties. The remarks made by the representatives at yesterday's reception are recorded as follows: 1. Fundamentally violating the law: Investigating changes to the tax system is the special prerogative of the central government. Unless it is approved by the Legislative Yuan and promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, it is not effective. The Guangdong Province local tobacco monopoly was an act of seizing profits from the people by high-pressure means during Chen Jitang's occupation and has no legal basis. Now that unification has been achieved, all illegal and harsh taxes in Guangdong Province are being gradually abolished. Only this monopoly continues to be implemented, which violates the central government's intention to start anew with the people of Guangdong. 2. Not in line with national conditions: At the beginning of the implementation of the monopoly, it was justified by the effective implementation in Germany and Japan, so it was imitated. How could they know that Japan initially had no tobacco production, so it used control to reject foreign imports? Germany also had insufficient supply to meet demand, so it used monopoly production and sales to stem leaks. Moreover, the tax systems of both countries are uniform, the political situation is on track, and social organizations are sound, capable of encouraging planting, mechanical manufacturing, and increasing production through collective farms, achieving the effect of collecting ample taxes and benefiting the people. Our country has a vast territory and only implements it in a corner of Guangdong Province. Guangdong farmers are scattered and plant separately, purely using manual manufacturing. The environment is completely different. How can we expect to reap its benefits? 3. Destroying production: Guangdong Province is an import-surplus province, relying on local tobacco production to slightly maintain the lifeline of the social economy. Now, since the monopoly has been in place for half a year, tobacco merchants have all been eliminated, and hundreds of thousands of workers who rely on this for a living have all become unemployed. In addition, the monopoly is taxed double the price (for example, if the value of the goods is 50 yuan, a tax of 50 yuan is levied, plus a monopoly fee of 1.6%). Merchants' costs increase, making sales difficult. Tobacco merchants are also struggling to survive. As a result of the drawbacks, domestic tobacco will inevitably gradually decline. 4. Unique tax system: Investigating the regulations for the collection of tobacco and alcohol taxes in the seven provinces promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, the maximum shall not exceed 30% of the value. In the past, local tobacco in Guangdong Province had already been taxed more than 140% of the value, with the heaviest burden in the country. Now, the monopoly has intensified, with officials seizing private enterprises, and taxes are levied at 100% of the value, treating a corner of Guangdong Province as outside of civilization, using it as a testing ground for new policies. How can this be said to be fair when considering the central government's unified tax system laws? The above are just a few of the major points. Other various malpractices are difficult to enumerate, directly undermining commerce and indirectly reducing tax sources. Therefore, Chairman Chiang's instructions in Guangdong also emphasized the absolute elimination of control and monopolies that compete with the people for profits, expressing his intention three times, which is clear evidence. Shanghai is the commercial center of our country, and the press especially wields the authority of national public opinion. We hope that you will impartially criticize this legacy of the warlords and urge the government to listen to public opinion and abolish it as soon as possible to alleviate the people's difficulties. The people of Guangdong will be fortunate.

Income Tax Has Been Collected for a Month; The Ministry of Finance Announces the Payment of Taxes; Various Agencies and Banks in This City Comply with the Order to Settle and Pay; The Bankers' Association Notifies Preparations for the Collection of Savings Interest Tax

The Income Tax Affairs Office of the Ministry of Finance has announced the payment of taxes after one month since the collection of income tax on salaries and compensation of public officials and interest on securities began on October 1. Various agencies in this city will report and remit the taxes. The Bankers' Association has been ordered to notify various banks to actively prepare for the procedures for collecting income tax on savings interest. The details are recorded as follows:

Ministry of Finance Announcement

The Income Tax Affairs Office of the Ministry of Finance issued Announcement No. 470 yesterday, stating, "It is found that income tax is now being collected. All local taxes should be uniformly paid to the local Central Bank for verification and receipt. In places without a Central Bank, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, as well as the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, have been entrusted by the bank to jointly handle the matter. In places without the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, or the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, other collection agencies have also been entrusted by the Central Bank to collect the taxes. Taxpayers are requested to directly pay to the aforementioned places in their local area. This is a special announcement."

Association Notice

The Bankers' Association of this city notified various banks in a letter yesterday, stating, "To whom it may concern, We have recently received Letter No. 349 from the Income Tax Affairs Office of the Ministry of Finance, stating, 'It is found that the Shanghai Bankers' Association previously submitted a request to the Ministry to postpone the collection of income tax on third-class savings interest. The Ministry has presented it to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government, which approved the postponement of the collection to January 1, 1937, and notified all relevant parties. Now that there are only two months until the collection date, all procedures should be actively prepared to ensure that the collection can begin on schedule and avoid delays. In addition to separate letters, we hereby request that you check and inform all colleagues and branch offices to implement this matter in a practical manner, etc.' Upon receiving this, we hereby inform all banks, hoping that you will check and comply." After receiving the letters, various banks immediately notified their branch offices to comply.

Payment of Taxes

After being ordered to collect income tax on salaries and compensation of public officials, various agencies in this city were visited by personnel from the Income Tax Affairs Office of the Ministry of Finance, who came to Shanghai to discuss the collection procedures and issued collection guidelines and forms, etc. Therefore, the collection was quite convenient for various agencies. Now that the collection period has been one month, according to regulations, taxes must be paid monthly. Currently, the heads of various agencies are instructing their accounting staff to deduct the taxes payable by all public officials for October in accordance with the regulations, prepare a list of taxpayers, and remit the taxes to the Central Bank, which collects the taxes, for reporting and payment to the national treasury. Various banks and money houses that have settled the income tax on government bond interest have also withheld and paid the taxes in accordance with the law. As for the total amount of income tax paid by various agencies and banks in this city, as the payments have not yet been completed, the office stationed by the Income Tax Affairs Office has no statistics yet.

Five Measures for Mr. Duan's Funeral Arrangements

The Duan Ziquan Funeral Office and Mr. Duan's family held a joint meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the funeral arrangements and agreed on five measures: (1) The Funeral Office will be established soon and will be divided into groups to handle affairs. (2) Funeral expenses will be in accordance with Mr. Duan's will, keeping everything frugal. (3) In accordance with Mr. Duan's will, no obituary will be issued, only public announcements in newspapers. (4) The wake will be held on December 6. (5) The coffin will be temporarily placed in the Shanghai residence until the National Funeral Office is established, and then a decision will be made.

After Mr. Duan Qirui's death, the central government has decided to hold a national funeral. Therefore, regarding the future burial site of Mr. Duan, the possibility of the Western Hills is greater, and it is unlikely to be buried in Shanghai or Beijing, and Hefei is also unlikely. Ping An Company's Baohua Steamer Robbed by Pirates Outside Wusong Estuary; No Passengers Spared; A Stray Bullet Grazed One Passenger; Carried the Loot to Yaguo Port in Chongming and Boarded a Sailboat to Escape; The Company Telegraphed the Military and Police Authorities to Strictly Pursue the Pirates

The Ping An Company's Baohua Steamer, sailing from Shanghai to Qidong, the shipowner is Wang Yunfa, and the comprador is Dong Chunfang, departed from Shanghai to Chongming Qidong at 5:00 p.m. on the sixth. Because the Xinren and other ships were not open due to furnace repairs, the Baohua was very crowded when it set sail, with a total of more than 500 passengers. Pirates boarded the ship in Shanghai posing as passengers. There were a total of sixteen pirates. When they were on the ship, most of them wore magnificent clothes, woolen hats, and glasses, and lived in the common cabin. There were many people on the ship, and no one paid attention. At 7:30 p.m., the ship had reached outside Wusong. Dinner was being served on the ship, and the crew and passengers were preparing to sleep after dinner. At this time, suddenly four or five pirates wandered back and forth inside and outside the cabin, looking around. The crew still regarded them as pickpockets and told them to be careful.

Surrounding the Maritime Police

The ship had two escorting police officers from the Qingtiantian warship in Haimen to protect it. At 7:30 p.m., the two police officers were having dinner in their room. Unexpectedly, the pirates had been paying attention to them for a long time. Taking advantage of their unpreparedness, two bandits suddenly opened fire with a pistol in front of the marine police cabin and immediately rushed in, forcing the two police officers to hand over their guns, otherwise they would be killed. The two police officers said they had no guns. One police officer resisted slightly and was beaten with a gun butt by a bandit, suffering minor injuries. Finally, the two bandits searched the marine police room and found one pistol and one box cannon, and 50 bullets, all of which were copied.

Robbery Situation

There were sixteen pirates, eight of whom had guns, half of whom spoke in local dialect, and half of whom spoke in the North Shazhou dialect. When they started at 7:30 p.m., the pirates took off their long clothes and changed into short clothes. While surrounding the marine police, two bandits went to the driver's platform to monitor the shipowner Wang Yunfa, who personally led the port and drove the ship. At the same time, two bandits went to the machine room to manage the engine, indicating that the bandits also had maritime talents. Two other bandits saw that the accounting room had finished collecting tickets and the room was counting banknotes. The two bandits immediately opened fire on it, breaking the glass door of the accounting room, and the bullet grazed a passenger. The bandits immediately entered and forced the accounting room to hand over all the cash.

Total Losses

More than 460 yuan in cash tickets were robbed from the accounting room, as well as 80 yuan in remittances carried by passengers. The crew's clothes, belongings, and private funds, and the cash from the ship's tea room were all searched. As for the passengers, the bandits first drove the passengers from the cabins to the lower cabin. When they arrived in the lower cabin, they searched each person one by one, robbed them of cash and belongings, and then escorted them to the cargo hold and locked everyone up. Passengers in the second and fourth cabins had about 1,100 yuan in wedding gifts and decorations, and a passenger surnamed Yan had 500 yuan, all of which were robbed. The losses of the remaining 500 passengers were no less than 1,000 yuan. The total loss is estimated at around 4,000 yuan.

Sated Loot and Escape

The pirates started robbing from 7:30 p.m. to 11:00 p.m. After the robbery was over, the ship had reached the sea near Yaguo Port. The pirates immediately dropped anchor and stopped the ship. The pirates then burned the "Lauterbach book" (a record of navigation for the shipping bureau) in the shipowner's room as a signal. Immediately, two pre-arranged punts came and shouted, "Is this the Xinren He Steamer?" The pirates said, "This is the Baohua. Our goal has been achieved." The punts then approached, and the pirates carried the loot onto the boat. The pirates then boarded the punts one after another. Before leaving, they fired two more shots with pistols to demonstrate and escape.

The Ship Returns to Shanghai

When the pirates were about to leave, they forced the crew to break off a screw from the cylinder head in the machine room, took one, and said they would borrow it for a while. After taking it, they threw it into the sea, and the Baohua Steamer could not travel. Before leaving, they also said to the ship's accountant, "When you get to Shanghai, if the newspapers come to inquire, tell them that the loss was only 2,000 yuan. Don't say too much about the amount. Our business this time was not bad." After the pirates left, the crew tried to fix the cylinder head with lead skin after seven hours of effort. They were able to sail until yesterday morning, but it was difficult to go to Chongming, so they had to return to Shanghai. At 12:15 noon yesterday, they finally arrived in Shanghai. The captain reported to the company, and the passengers who had been robbed also went ashore. The ship needs to repair the cylinder and is currently docked at the Nanshi Pier.

Telegraphs for Arresting Thieves

After arriving in Shanghai, shipowner Wang and comprador Dong went to the Shanghai Company at 214 Nanshi Wai Ma Road and reported the incident to General Manager Dong Lianchen, Manager Li Yaoting, and Assistant Manager Chen Yisheng. The General Manager immediately submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications, the Shanghai Shipping Bureau, the Shanghai Steamer Industry Association, and the Jianghai Customs Maritime Public Security Bureau. In addition to reporting the incident, he also requested strict arrest of the pirates to protect the safety of passengers. He also telegraphed the military and police agencies in Chongming, Qidong, and Haimen counties, requesting strict arrest of the pirates.

Fisheries Syndicate Established Preparatory Office Yesterday; Capital of One Million; Banks Have Committed 800,000; The Remaining 200,000 Will Be Requested by the Ministry of Industry from the Ministry of Finance

The Fisheries Syndicate, jointly established by the Ministry of Industry and the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and other banks, established a preparatory office yesterday afternoon. Each bank committed funds, and Qian Xinzhi and others were appointed as preparatory committee members. After the procedures are completed, it will be formally established. A reporter from the Central News Agency learned the details and recorded them below:

Consultations Yesterday Afternoon

Twelve banks are participating in the Fisheries Syndicate, including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, the Jin Cheng Bank, the Dalu Bank, the Yanye Bank, the Zhongnan Bank, the Si Ming Bank, the Zhonghui Bank, the Xinhua Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association. The Ministry of Industry sent a letter requesting Qian Xinzhi, Wang Zhixin, and Dong Yanfang to prepare. A draft plan has been drawn up, and a luncheon was held at the Bank Club yesterday afternoon to discuss the progress, attended by representatives from each bank, including Cheng Muhao, Wang Shaoxian, Dong Chengdao, Wang Zhixin, Qian Xinzhi, Yang Weichang, Zhou Desun, Cao Jiru, Chen Guangting, Jin Caisheng, etc. Qian Xinzhi was unanimously elected as the temporary chairman.

Preparations

During the meeting, Qian Xinzhi first reported on the progress of the preparations, stating that the Ministry of Industry, in view of the decline of the fishing industry in recent years, proposed the organization of a Fisheries Syndicate to engage in relief. This spring, Minister Wu reported at a tea party with bankers in Shanghai, which was approved by all the banks. The Ministry also drafted an outline, which was approved by the Executive Yuan meeting. A total of twelve banks participated at that time, and Wang Zhixin and Yang Yanfang and this person were responsible for the preparations. At that time, because the various rules and regulations were still being drafted, the establishment was delayed. However, the fishermen urgently needed relief because the winter fishing season was approaching, so the three banks first raised 120,000 yuan and lent them separately to the Yinxian Fisheries Cooperative and the wholesalers of the fish market, who then lent them to the fishing boats. A special report was attached.

Capital Commitment

The syndicate's capital is set at 1 million yuan, with the Ministry of Industry undertaking 200,000 yuan, and a letter has been sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting allocation. The other 800,000 yuan will be undertaken by each bank. It was decided on the spot yesterday to divide it into 40 shares, with each share being 20,000 yuan. The Bank of China and the Bank of Communications jointly subscribed for 11 shares (220,000 yuan). Si Ming subscribed for 2 shares (40,000 yuan). Shanghai, Dalu, Jin Cheng, Yanye, Zhongnan, Zhejiang Industrial, Zhonghui, Xinhua, and the Four Banks Savings Association each subscribed for 3 shares (60,000 yuan each), totaling 40 shares, totaling 800,000 yuan. It was also decided to continue to appoint Qian, Wang, and Wei as preparatory committee members, with Qian Xinzhi as the convener. The preparatory office will be established immediately, and after several more meetings, the syndicate can be formally established and will begin lending in the spring fishing season next year.

Minister of Railways, Mr. Zhang Gongquan's Speech: How Employees Should Strive to Fulfill Their National Defense Responsibilities

Shanghai News Agency: Railway Minister Zhang Gongquan arrived in Shanghai from Beijing some time ago. At the invitation of the Railway Employees' Military Training Class, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency recorded his speech as follows: Fellow railway employees, you are here today for training. I believe that when you first arrived, each of you must have had a thought in mind: "We are serving the railways, why do we need to come here for training? Military affairs are the business of soldiers, what does it have to do with railway employees?" Therefore, I would like to take this opportunity of the belated opening ceremony to solemnly say to you:

Railway Enterprise

In peacetime, it is the lifeline of transportation; in wartime, it is a sharp weapon for marching troops. Therefore, I have often said that the railway enterprise is a business of peace and also a business of war. Therefore, your training here today is directly for military training, and indirectly for your own careers, and to fulfill your own duties. There should be no special or unusual feelings about this. Furthermore, we who serve the railways must deeply understand the railway's responsibility to the nation.

Responsibilities in Three Areas

(1) Facilitating Passengers: We must ensure that the people of the whole country understand the convenience of railway transportation, sweep away the previous concept of "viewing travel as a fearful journey," and make everyone happy to travel. It must be understood that the people's concept of patriotism has a great relationship with travel. Travel can appreciate the beauty of the country's rivers and mountains, recognize the greatness of the nation, draw inspiration from the beauty of the mountains and forests, enlighten wisdom, and increase empathy through the influence of the eyes and ears. People's thoughts can be communicated, and feelings of brotherhood can be strengthened. Thus, mutual assistance and cooperation can be achieved. Mutual assistance and unity come first, and cooperation is the foundation of national salvation. Therefore, our efforts to facilitate passengers can be said to be work that enhances cooperation, friendship, and unity among the people, and inspires their patriotism and national salvation concepts. It is not just fulfilling the duties of railway employees themselves. (2) Smooth Cargo Transportation: "Smooth flow of goods" is the legacy of Mr. Sun Yat-sen and the essence of people's livelihood. However, how to transport goods from the inland to various places in the fastest and most economical way is the inescapable responsibility of our railway employees. Because after the smooth flow of goods, not only can our daily needs be met domestically, without having to rely on foreign sources, but we can also take a step further to supply the people with genuine and inexpensive goods, so that living expenses do not rise, and to make practical improvements to the overall national economy. (3) Facilitating Military Transportation: The organization of the military is like a machine, and railway transportation is a gear in this machine. As the art of war says, "Speed is of the essence in war." How to ensure that the transportation of troops and military supplies does not miss the opportunity is the responsibility of the railway. Therefore, the railway should always study equipment and train employees in peacetime, and prepare both materially and spiritually, so that its facilities can fulfill the function of military transportation. This is also the task undertaken by all railway employees. The first two are what should be paid attention to in peacetime, and the latter is what should be strived for in wartime. If we talk about the importance of national security, the latter should be the priority. Because the people must first live in peace and then enjoy their work, and only by enjoying their work can there be production and travel. If they cannot live in peace and enjoy their work, where will the transportation of goods come from? What leisure will there be for travel? Therefore, how to strengthen national power and

Consolidate National Defense

So that the people can live and work in peace is the prerequisite for fulfilling all responsibilities. However, when "national defense" is mentioned, it is often regarded as the business of the military. It is not known that the nation is an accumulation of people. Only when everyone can do their best in their own jobs can we talk about national defense. Only when everyone can serve the country can national defense be strengthened. Therefore, national defense is the responsibility of all citizens, regardless of gender, age, or status, inside and out. It cannot and must not be shirked to others. As the sages said, "Everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." However, how to fulfill the responsibility of citizens is not only something that everyone can talk about and know, but must also be practiced and implemented. Knowing without acting is equal to not knowing. The way to implement it is to embrace the idea of "the nation is supreme" and dedicate all our energy to the interests of the entire nation, sacrificing the individual for the sake of the greater good. To put it another way, we who serve the railways must identify our goals and fulfill our duties. Once an emergency occurs, we must be determined to

Devote Efforts to Military Support

And sacrifice for the country without hesitation. If we can do this, we will not fail the mission of railway employees, and we will be able to fulfill the responsibilities of citizens. At present, the international situation is tense, and all countries have established emergency agencies to prevent emergencies. For example, in the Soviet Union, railway employees are all members of the National Defense Assistance Association, which aims to popularize national defense ideas and implement military training, so that railway employees and the rear civilian population can join hands and work together to contribute to military education outside of the military, such as transportation, propaganda, air defense, and anti-poisoning. At present, this National Defense Assistance Association has become the most powerful organization in the Soviet Union's semi-military organization. The total number of members reaches more than 12 million, and railway employees account for 60 percent of them. Other organizations, such as the Military Knowledge Research Association and the Shooting Research Association, have very strict facilities for military education and military training, and railway employees are the most important members. This is because the relationship between railways and national defense is the closest. Once war breaks out, how to quickly and safely transport personnel, horses, grain, and ammunition according to the battle plan, and concentrate them at designated locations, is the most important thing in combat. In addition, the evacuation of wounded soldiers, the protection of refugees from the war zone, and the supply of military supplies must all rely on transportation agencies to adapt to the situation, so that they can be fully maintained and have the ability to sustain combat.

During the European War

The railway transportation in northern and eastern France, in just one day and night in 1915, dispatched 180 trains, 231 trains in 1916, and 267 trains in 1918. Due to the rapid transportation of military supplies, the combat capability of the expeditionary forces was ensured. The intensity of future wars will probably be several times greater than in the past. Therefore, military transportation will play an increasingly important role in war operations. Railway employees should think carefully about what important responsibilities they will bear for national defense. Our country does not yet have an organization similar to the National Defense Assistance Association. Your training here is to replace this work. (It must be known that our country is facing national crises, and the key to survival lies in self-reliance and regeneration. The way to regenerate is to be prepared for danger in times of peace and to prepare in time so that we can calmly deal with everything when emergencies come. It is important to know that the progress of the times is endless, and the responsibility of the railway also increases, changes, and becomes heavier with it. In the past, national mobilization involved at most hundreds of thousands of people. In the future, once something happens, it will involve hundreds of thousands of people. May I ask if we have this training now? Are we prepared for large-scale transportation? Can we truly take on the responsibility? In addition, with the advancement of modern science, the weapons of war are changing with each passing day. Naval, land, and air battles have moved from two-dimensional to three-dimensional competition. Therefore, military mobilization should be as fast as possible, and how to ensure safety during transportation. If we do not prepare seriously in advance, it cannot be arranged temporarily. Therefore, how to prepare effectively in terms of intelligence and equipment today is the responsibility of every railway employee. The occurrence of emergencies cannot be predicted. Once it happens, we must do our best and sacrifice ourselves to serve the country. We must also have comprehensive knowledge for the application of each department. Suppose the railway tracks are destroyed from the air, we cannot rely solely on the engineering and mechanical departments to be responsible for repairs. Everyone must have this ability to remedy it at any time. Then, when an emergency comes, one person can do the work of two, and one thing can be used for two purposes.

Modern warfare is not only a war of force, but also a war of manpower, material resources, and financial resources. In other words, it is also a war of whether every citizen can effectively fulfill their responsibilities. Therefore, I have endless feelings and endless expectations when I speak to you here today. I sincerely hope that you will not regard yourselves as mere railway employees. Everyone must regard themselves as one of the great citizens of the Republic of China. Whether in peace or war, we must be prepared and able to fulfill our responsibilities. I was not originally familiar with the railway business. Since I took on this role, I have known that the railway business is complex and confusing. I do not know where to start in order to fulfill its due mission. However, given the time and space in which the country finds itself today, national defense is the top priority. That is why I work tirelessly every day and strive for governance, lest I be too late. And that is why I hope you will be self-reliant, strive for excellence, and make greater progress today. It cannot be denied that there are shortcomings in the spirit and discipline of the various items at present. However, the transformation of the atmosphere depends on a few people taking the lead, advocating first, and then gradually influencing and promoting it to the public. You are here for training, and after the expiration, you will return to your respective roads to teach others what you have learned. Therefore, you are only a few hundred people here, but your responsibility and influence are really above thousands of people. I deeply hope that you will hold on to your ambition and restrain your emotions, recognize the beliefs we should have and the mission we should fulfill, and adhere to it and practice it, so that the responsibility of citizens can be fulfilled and the national crisis can be alleviated.

Lake Society Telegraphs the Zhejiang Provincial Government to Vigorously Suppress the Communist Bandits in Xiaofeng

The Lake Society recently telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government, saying: "According to a letter from our fellow townsman Xu Manxin, Xiaofeng is located in a mountainous rural area. Recently (in the past month), there have been about 400 Communist bandits occupying the southwest townships, acting arbitrarily, and the villagers cannot bear the poison. Within a radius of more than a hundred miles, the population is almost extinct. Those with a little status have taken refuge in towns, Meixi, or Huzhou. These Communist bandits are organized in a very tight manner. Due to the vigorous suppression in Ningguo and other counties in Anhui, some of them fled into Xiaofeng. Although there are local defense regiments and a small number of provincial security teams to encircle and suppress them, they are ultimately unable to achieve success due to the small number of people and incomplete firearms. The bandits arbitrarily rob everywhere. The village chiefs,保 chiefs, or 甲 chiefs are either kidnapped or shot. If they have any property, they are kidnapped for ransom. They are equipped with firearms and are located in the deep mountains, so it may not be easy to encircle and suppress them without a large army. If this continues, it will spread, and not only Xiaofeng County's life and property will be harmed. Therefore, we sincerely state the actual situation and request that you immediately telegraph the provincial government to send a large army to encircle and suppress them, so as to eliminate them as soon as possible, which is the blessing of our fellow townsmen." Upon receiving the information, the Society found that Xiaofeng borders Anhui Province, and the mountains are intertwined, which has always been a den for bandits. This time, the Communist bandits disturbed the people, and if they are not vigorously suppressed soon, they will spread to neighboring towns. Therefore, we specially telegraph you, asking you to immediately transfer to the Security Department to send troops to encircle and suppress them, in order to maintain security. We are compelled to make this statement and hope you will consider it. Chen Qicai, Chairman of the Lake Society Committee, bows, fish.

Tao Guilin Discusses the Cement Price Increase Problem

A reporter from the Central News Agency saw a report in the newspaper yesterday about the current state of cement companies' business and specially visited Mr. Tao Guilin of the construction industry. According to his views, the cement manufacturers have recently raised prices twice, and the total price per barrel has reached more than six yuan. The reason is unknown. However, according to the market price in the 24th year of the Republic (the average price per barrel in the first half of the 24th year was 5.5 yuan, and the average price per barrel in the second half was 3.5 yuan), the average was only 4.5 yuan. However, the China Cement Company's year-end settlement report shows that in addition to the government profit, dividend, and depreciation, a large amount has been proposed, and there is still a sufficient surplus. Judging from the actual situation, the cement cost and selling price of 4.5 yuan may be an appropriate number. Compared with the current price and the price last year, the difference is very high. What is the reason? I dare not say. Recently, the sales volume of cement has increased sharply, mostly due to the needs of national construction. I believe that cement manufacturers should increase their production to meet the demand, and the cost can be reduced due to the increase in production, so as to reduce the government's burden. If cement manufacturers take the opportunity to raise prices, the country will directly bear a heavy burden, and our industry will indirectly suffer intangible losses. However, since we are all Chinese people, there is no worry about external leakage. However, in this critical period, our industry is very willing to help each other with cement manufacturers, share the same boat, and serve the country. This is my wish, or it may be the enthusiasm of all compatriots in the country. Finally, Mr. Tao hopes that cement manufacturers can have an appropriate standard pricing to avoid inconsistent prices, so that the construction industry can also obtain a price guarantee.

New Factory Inspection Measures

An overseas news agency translated a report from the mainland, saying that regarding the factory inspection problem in the Special Zone, it was recently heard that the Ministry of Industry, following the wishes of the Municipal Council, has drafted implementation rules in accordance with the Chinese Factory Law, which is expected to solve the problem. The Municipal Government of this city will follow the government's instructions and continue to negotiate with the Municipal Council authorities based on the points agreed upon by both parties. However, all the details of this issue are currently lacking formal reports. The Ministry of Industry's agreement to the Municipal Council's proposal should open a new path for the future of negotiations on the previous draft that was rejected by the consular body. According to the proposal, Municipal Council Director General Fessenden suggested to Municipal Government Secretary Yu Hongjun, hoping to ease the differences between the Chinese side's territorial sovereignty and the various countries' consular jurisdiction. According to the consular body's statement opposing the draft, the implementation of the Chinese Factory Law on foreigners enjoying consular jurisdiction is tantamount to hindering the rights that should be enjoyed under the treaty. However, the Chinese side believes that factory inspection is a Chinese administrative right and cannot allow any treaty country's consular jurisdiction to infringe upon it. In order to ease this difference, Fessenden suggested that the Municipal Council, based on the Chinese Factory Law, draft its own implementation rules for inspection and list them as one of the regulations. All factories in the area, regardless of the nationality of the factory owner, should be implemented uniformly. In this way, the Municipal Council can implement the management of industrial institutions within its own scope of authority. In addition to this technical change, other rules obtained by the Yu and Liang after five years of negotiation have not been changed. At present, the measures proposed by the Municipal Council are the same as those stipulated in the draft rejected by the consular body. The implementation of the inspection rules will be carried out by personnel with equal numbers of Chinese and foreigners. The new measures were previously considered by the Ministry of Industry and then by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Executive Yuan.

First Special District Bailiff Miao Changzhen Accused: Who Altered the Receipt? Qian Xingcun Claims Li Pu Told Him About the Alteration and Excessive Collection; Defense Lawyer Lists Li Pu's Past Facts

Miao Changzhen from Zhenjiang, a bailiff in the First Special District Court, 29 years old, residing at No. 63 Yongqing Lane, Love Lane, was accused of altering the delivery fee of eight cents to two yuan and eight cents when he was ordered to deliver a payment order to Qian Xingcun on the upper floor of Wanfeng Sauce Garden, No. 499 Fangbang Road, on the 28th of last month. Qian reported him to the Procuratorate of the First Special District Court. Prosecutor Song Genshan opened a court to investigate and concluded the investigation, took Miao into custody, and filed a public prosecution with the same-level court for the crimes of fraud, alteration of official documents, and dereliction of duty. Miao Changzhen was a public official and should have his original sentence increased in accordance with Article 134 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide opened a criminal court to hear the case. The defendant Miao Changzhen hired lawyer Li Lin to appear in court as his defense. Miao Changzhen stated that he was a bailiff in the First Special District Court. On the 28th of last month, he was ordered to deliver a payment order to Wanfeng Sauce Garden, No. 499 Fangbang Road, and handed it to a person. However, he did not ask whether the recipient was Qian Xingcun at the time. The recipient paid him a delivery fee of eight cents in silver. The receipt now shows a figure of one yuan and eight cents. He does not know who filled in this figure. He only received eight cents at the time. At this point, his defense lawyer Li Lin said that the lawyer had investigated the case at the Shenxiangge Public Security Bureau. There is no Qian Xingcun on the household registration record at No. 499 Fangbang Road. The person who filed the report with the court was actually Li Pu, also known as Li Jinqing. The matter was instigated and provoked by Li Pu. Li passed the Second Judicial District Bailiff Examination and was a candidate for bailiff, but he has not been appointed to a substantive vacancy. If one of the bailiffs in the court is transferred, he hopes to be appointed to a substantive vacancy. Li Pu is currently an employee of the Yangtze Hotel and often represents litigants in court. His home is on the upper floor of the sauce garden at No. 499 Fangbang Road. He is actually a litigator. This point should be noted. Furthermore, if the defendant did forge official documents and defraud Qian Xingcun, he would definitely use the same method on Kangren, the opposing party of Qian Xingcun. The lawyer has obtained the delivery receipt of the opposing party and it has not been altered, which is submitted as evidence in rebuttal. Qian Xingcun stated that he was 41 years old, from Huzhou, and engaged in the silk business. He lived on the upper floor of the sauce garden at No. 499 Fangbang Road. Li Pu is his brother-in-law. His sister Qian Acan is married to Li as his wife, so he lives with Li. When the defendant delivered the payment order and collected a delivery fee of one yuan and eight cents, he was out. Later, Li Pu told him that there was an altered receipt and an overcharge of one yuan. Therefore, Li drafted a report and reported it to the court for investigation. Pan Shizhong, a clerk in the First Special District Court, testified that the figure of one yuan on the delivery receipt was added by someone else. Witness Zhu Dianyuan stated that he was an apprentice in Wanfeng Sauce Garden and testified that he代收 the payment order and 代钱 sign. At the time, because he saw that the receipt stated one yuan and eight cents, he asked Zhu Zhenfang, Li Pu's wife, for the money. Zhu first took out eight cents in silver and twelve cents in small coins, which he handed over. Later, because the person who came to collect the money did not accept small coins, he exchanged them for a one-dollar bill. He could not remember whether the person was the defendant, but his height and hair were not similar. Witness woman Zhu Zhenfang testified that Li Pu is her husband and Qian Xingcun's wife is her sister. That day, Zhu Dianyuan代收 the document and said that it required one yuan and eight cents. She took down a nickel coin of one yuan and eight cents from upstairs and asked Zhu to hand it over. Later, because the person who came to collect the money did not accept it, Zhu Dianyuan asked the sauce garden accounting room to exchange the nickel coin for a one-dollar bill. Finally, the defendant's lawyer stated that Li Pu had also accused three bailiffs, Wang Liang, Gong Kuan, etc., in the Second Special District Court last year. He requested an investigation into this point to prove Li's character. Judge Feng ruled that the case still needed to be investigated, ordered the defendant to be returned to custody, and rescheduled the hearing for next Tuesday.

The United General Office of the World Red Swastika Society of China's Southeast Branches, in response to the outbreak of malignant malaria in Rugao, Nantong Dongchen, Liyang, Jurong, Changzhou, Jiangsu Province, which caused numerous deaths, has already sent circulars to various branches, urging them to quickly find ways to provide relief. It is now learned that the society has organized a malaria eradication team in Nantong Rugao and three teams in the Dongchen branch, and four teams in the Changzhou branch. Robbers Acted Calmly Last Night, Major Robbery Case on Fenzhou Road, Jinchang Sand Casting Suffered Heavy Losses, Four Robbers Searched and Robbed with Guns, Called Xiang Sheng Taxi to Escape, Police are Investigating Intensively

Cao Weiyang from Hubei, who works in sand casting, opened the Cao Jinchang Sand Casting Shop at No. 16, Fenzhou Lane (intersection of Fenzhou Road and Yangzhou Road). Because he had some savings, he was targeted by robbers. At about 9:40 p.m. last night, while Cao Weiyang was taking a bath in the bathhouse, four robbers suddenly came to his house. They were wearing long black cloth gowns, long magenta woolen gowns, and short blue cloth jackets. Two robbers held handguns, and two robbers held sharp axes. They first knocked on the door and falsely claimed to be visiting Cao Laoban. Then they reached in and pulled out the door bolt and rushed in. First, they drove the apprentices in the shop to the second-floor loft and locked them up. Then, they locked the men and women on the second and third floors together in the living room on the second floor, forbidding them to make any noise, and sent one robber to guard them with a gun. The remaining robbers went straight to the third floor, broke into Cao's bedroom, and began to search and rob, turning over boxes and cabinets. Around 10:20 p.m., the three robbers retreated, carrying out a large leather suitcase and two handheld suitcases, and took them downstairs to the living room. At the same time, one robber used the sand casting shop's own telephone to call the Xiang Sheng Taxi Company, instructing them to send a car to Yangzhou Road to wait, and asked someone to greet them there. The robbers also told the Xiang Sheng Taxi Company that the person hiring the car was from No. 16, Fenzhou Lane, and the telephone number was 53222. After finishing speaking, they hung up the phone. One robber went outside to wait for the car. After receiving the call, the Xiang Sheng Company immediately notified the 18th branch station on Huade Road and dispatched taxi No. 18476 to provide service. Upon arriving at Yangzhou Road, someone was indeed greeting them and instructed the driver to wait a moment. The robber returned to No. 16 with the other three robbers, carried out the three suitcases, put them in the car, and sped away. By the time the apprentices regained their freedom and tracked them out of the lane, the robbers had already disappeared. They immediately telegraphed the Yulin Road Police Station to report, and the police sent detectives to investigate. They also inquired with the Xiang Sheng Taxi Company about the license plate number of the car hired from No. 16, telegraphed various police agencies, and requested their cooperation in apprehending the robbers. At around 11:30 p.m., the car was indeed discovered on the Bund of Edward Road and was immediately impounded. It was learned that the robbers had gotten off near Mintini Alley in the French Concession. At the time, the driver did not know that he was carrying robbers. After the patrol officer informed him of the case, he was taken to the police station and transferred to Yulin Road for investigation. Meanwhile, the loss was investigated. It was reported that nine gold rings, three gemstone rings, one gold watch, two women's watches, three pairs of gold bracelets, and one silver dollar were robbed. All the leather clothing and more expensive clothes were stored in the three suitcases and taken away, with a great value. Afterwards, according to neighbors, two of the four robbers had very familiar faces and all had pockmarks. The fact that the robbers dared to act so calmly and hire a car to escape after the robbery is truly an innovation in robbery cases. Therefore, the police are now sending detectives everywhere, rigorously searching for the robbers' tracks, and striving to arrest them and solve the case as soon as possible.

Fashion Workers' Strike, Fifteen People Sentenced for Obstructing Bodily Injury and Freedom, Fourteen Detained, One Imprisoned

Due to wage reductions and other issues by employers and foremen in various fashion stores in this city, a general strike was triggered, which has lasted for several days.
