Chinese and Western detectives from the police station rushed to suppress the situation and arrested the rioting workers, including (1) Wu Jinzhang, (2) Chen Rongcai, (3) Qian Zhongbao, (4) Chen Hongpin, (5) Wei Youcai, (6) Wang Shukun, (7) Lu Hehong, (8) Yu Ajun, (9) Zhang Asan, (10) Zai Maosong, (11) Luo Zhiting, (12) Jiang Guoman, (13) Tong Shaofu, (14) Zhang Along, (15) Chen Zongjie, along with the weapon, a washboard, and detained them in the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu filed a lawsuit in accordance with Article 304 of the Criminal Law, obstruction of freedom, and stated the case, saying that at 11:30 a.m. yesterday, the first to sixth defendants, along with many others, broke into the Xinguang Clothing Store at No. 200, Hubei Road, and demanded that the foreman Lu A'gen and the other eighteen workers join the strike and increase wages. They immediately threatened violence. Lu A'gen stated that the employer of this store did not deduct wages and expressed unwillingness to accept. The group then wanted to commit violence. Lu, seeing the situation was not good, escaped from the back door. The group chased after him, beating him with fists and wooden sticks. The first defendant threw a washboard at him, causing injuries to Lu's head and back. Lu immediately grabbed the first defendant and called for help from patrol officers No. 2359, who arrested the first to sixth defendants. More than ten others escaped. The seventh to tenth defendants broke into the Dachina Fashion Store at No. 704, Hankou Road, at around 2:00 p.m. yesterday, inciting the strike. The foreman Qiao Zhenfang, seeing that there were many people and the situation was overwhelming, immediately stopped work. He went to the store, and the group suspected that Qiao was going out to report to the police, so they rushed into the factory, wantonly making trouble, and throwing tables and other objects outside. The Chinese police arrested the seventh defendant. While taking him to the Laozao Police Station, when passing near the Yangtze Hotel on Yunnan Road, the eighth defendant and others followed behind, shouting "Beat the patrol officer." The Chinese police arrested the eighth defendant. Unexpectedly, the ninth and tenth defendants, disregarding the law, continued to shout and incite passersby, intending to snatch the arrested suspect. The ninth and tenth defendants were arrested and taken to the police station. The remaining eleventh to fourteenth defendants, at 2:10 p.m. yesterday, after the Dachina case occurred, because some workers returned to the store, intending to continue working, a group of strikers rushed into the store again, dragged the worker Lu Fulin out, intending to drag him to the Garment Union at No. 15, Lane 614, Fuzhou Road. He was arrested on Hankou Road and Guangxi Road. The fifteenth defendant dragged the worker Ni Songfei into the union, beat him, and dragged him from the union to Yuqiaqing Road, where he was arrested. Therefore, Ni suffered internal injuries. In view of this type of case, which has occurred frequently recently, the Municipal Council believes that the defendants are making unreasonable demands, disrupting the security of the concession, and the situation is serious, and should be severely punished. According to the testimonies of witnesses Lu A'gen, Lu Fulin, and Ni Songfei, the defendants Wu Jinzhang and others hired lawyer Fan Gang to appear in court as their defense. After the court investigation by Ye Shengchao, the defendants were sentenced. The court sentenced the first to sixth defendants to 50 days of detention for jointly injuring others, the seventh to tenth defendants to 40 days of detention for jointly coercing and obstructing others from exercising their rights, the eleventh to fourteenth defendants to 50 days of detention for jointly detaining and depriving others of their freedom of action, and the fifteenth defendant to two months of imprisonment for the same crime.

Tram Conductor Attempted Suicide by Drowning, Saved and Not Beheaded

Zhu Huiren, No. 330, a ticket seller of the Public Concession Tram Company, 41 years old, lived at No. 3, Linhe Lane, Huishan Road. Yesterday (the 7th) at about 11:30 a.m., he wandered on the bank of the Suzhou River at the south end of the Zhabu Road Bridge. Suddenly, he jumped into the river, attempting suicide. A boatman heard the sound and immediately rescued him, preventing him from being submerged. Later, someone reported to the patrolling Chinese patrol officer No. 3389, who took him to the Central Police Station and transferred him to Renji Hospital for treatment. Under questioning by the police chief, he confessed that he was falsely accused by ticket inspector No. 127 of the company, which led to his dismissal. He had been working for the tram company for more than ten years, and now he had come to such an end, he had no face, and he had a 73-year-old mother above and a wife and children below, and he had no savings, and life was so difficult, he thought it was better to die.

Foreign Car Injured Couple, Disaster Struck on the Way Back from Sightseeing, Indian Patrol Officer Saw Them Bleeding

Zhang Liying, an actor, 31 years old, from Beijing, has been performing in Kaifeng. At the beginning of this month, he and his wife, Ms. Ma, 23 years old, set off for Shanghai and resided at No. 4, Xinglongfang, Chongqing Road. Last night, Zhang and Ms. Ma, having long heard of the prosperity of Shanghai, went out for sightseeing. They strolled along and arrived at the Garden Bridge. The two looked out over the scenery of the Huangpu River. Then they turned back and intended to return home. Unexpectedly, at this time, a Westerner, E.M. Artis, residing at No. 885, Broadway Road, drove his private car, license No. 3787, from the north side of the bridge to the south at high speed. Zhang and Ms. Ma were walking in front of the car. They heard the sound of the car behind them and tried to avoid it, but it was too late. They were hit by the car and fell out for a great distance, and their heads were broken and bleeding. A nearby Indian patrol officer saw it and quickly impounded the car and took it to the police station for questioning. Zhang and Ms. Ma were sent to the Nursing Home and Guangren Hospital for treatment. However, Ms. Ma was only slightly injured and was discharged from the hospital.

Overseas Chinese from Singapore, Wang Zhensheng, Invents Kerosene Engine Car, Can Use Singapore Kerosene Instead of Gasoline, Because It Is Cheaper, Many People Like to Use It

According to the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation, Mr. Wang Zhensheng, the owner of Wang Zhensheng Company in Singapore, has invented a kerosene engine car that uses Singapore kerosene instead of gasoline. This type of car has been running in various cities of Chaozhou Prefecture for the past two years, and many people are using it. Many cargo trucks and private cars in Singapore are also equipped with it. However, long-distance passenger cars were not equipped because the Bureau of Motor Vehicles had not yet approved it. Those in the industry hope for approval, as using a kerosene engine can also save costs. Recently, the Bureau of Motor Vehicles has approved the installation of kerosene engines in long-distance passenger cars. As a result, car owners have been contacting Mr. Wang to switch to kerosene engines. Mr. Wang is now working day and night to rush production to meet the demand. According to recent news, Mr. Wang has also invented a new type of kerosene engine, which has faster speed and cleaner engine than the old type. It is the same as ordinary cars, and the magic lies in reducing fuel consumption. If the Singapore kerosene runs out on the way, it can be replaced by kerosene or gasoline.

French Municipal Council Announces Regulations for Transporting and Selling Goods

The French Concession Municipal Council has promulgated six regulations for transporting and selling certain goods from the Public Concession to the French Concession, and specially announced them to the attention of merchants in various industries. The full text of the general rules is as follows: Article 1: Any merchant or company established in the Public Concession who engages in the following businesses and wishes to sell its products in the French Concession shall first obtain approval from the Municipal Council. The foods include milk and milk by-products, edible oils and fats, bread, pastries, ice cream, edible ice, biscuits, candies, locally made alcoholic beverages, soft drinks without alcohol, beer, soy milk, and canned foods. Article 2: This sales notice shall be issued by the Bureau of Hygiene and Relief after a written request from the merchant and after investigation or inspection. This notice shall be renewed annually and shall be valid from January 1 to December 31. This notice may not be transferred. The fee is determined annually. Article 3: Delivery personnel for businesses specified in Article 1 shall be required to hold a special card issued by the Bureau of Hygiene and Relief. This card shall state: 1. The name of the business operator; 2. The nature of the business and its location. This card shall be renewed annually and shall be valid from January 1 to December 31. If lost, a duplicate card may be issued. The value of each card shall be (see the tax schedule). Article 4: The Bureau shall have the right to inspect the places where the foods are manufactured, collected, or stored for which the notice is issued. This inspection shall be carried out by the Bureau of Hygiene and Relief jointly with the Public Concession Health Department. The Bureau may jointly carry out periodic inspections with the Public Concession Health Department and submit the following documents to the Public Works Department: 1. A list of merchants applying for a sales notice in the French Concession; 2. A list of merchants holding a sales notice in the French Concession. However, due to the special circumstances of dairy farms, any dairy farm established in the Public Concession that holds a sales notice in the French Concession may be inspected at any time by personnel from the French Concession Bureau of Hygiene and Relief. Article 5: The sales notice and card may be revoked by the French Consul General, and the Public Works Department of the Public Concession shall be notified of this ruling immediately. Any person who violates these regulations may be prosecuted by the Public Concession Public Works Department in the competent court. Article 6: Any person who operates a business specified in Article 1 in the French Concession and wishes to transport its products to the Public Concession for sale may, on the principle of reciprocity, be permitted by the Public Concession authorities to apply all of the above regulations. Chapter 6: Bureau of Hygiene and Relief, businesses established in the Public Concession, sales notice in the French Concession, 5 yuan per year; delivery in the French Concession, 1 yuan per card per year; 10 yuan per duplicate delivery card.

Corpse in Wooden Box at Pier No. 4 of the 16th Concession, Resembling a Discharged Soldier

In the afternoon of the previous day, at about 1:00 p.m., a large wooden box was found at Pier No. 4 of the 16th Concession in Nanshi. Inside was the unidentified corpse of a man wearing old military uniforms, resembling a discharged soldier. The local headman reported it to the local court. Yesterday morning, the prosecutor arrived at the scene to inspect it. There were no wounds on the body, and it was determined to be a natural death. Since there were no family members, the local headman was instructed to collect a coffin from the charity hall for burial in the public cemetery, pending identification.

Seduction and Reward – Xian Rongxiang’s Account of Seeking a Concubine

Jia Rongxiang, a 42-year-old man from Tianjin, operates the Shuanghe Xing Copper Shop at No. 10 Ningbo Road in the French Concession. Three years ago, he encountered Di Xiuying, also known as Wang Hongmei (22 years old this year), a woman from Liyang, in a brothel. They fell in love at first sight, and Jia took her as a concubine, living together in the shop. The elderly husband and young wife were deeply affectionate. Recently, due to the enticement of a neighbor, Ms. Di became disgusted with her husband's old age and weakness and had an affair. On the eighth of last month, taking advantage of Jia's return to his hometown in Tianjin, Di swept away all her clothes and over 1,900 yuan in cash, and secretly ran away. She and her lover rented a room in a hotel and lived together. When Jia returned to Shanghai and discovered this, he reported it to the French police and requested an investigation. He also posted a reward of 100 yuan in the newspaper to find the neighbor who instigated the affair. The neighbor, known as Mr. Jia, seeing that the scandal had been exposed, fearing involvement, pretended to help in the search and informed Ms. Di to return home. Mr. Jia received a reward of 100 yuan and 50 yuan for travel expenses from Jia, considering the matter settled. This was discovered by Qin Youyu, a detective of the French police, who detained Di Xiuying. She confessed her lover and the introducer. Yesterday, the police escorted Di to the Criminal Division 8 of the Special District Court. Judge Zhang Minsheng conducted the trial. The police prosecutor requested an extension for investigation and the arrest of the implicated parties. After the court questioned Ms. Di, the hearing was adjourned for fourteen days. The defendant was granted bail of 500 yuan with a shop as surety. If no surety was provided, she was to be remanded in custody.

Carpenter Lou Yunyan – Forging Permits for Extortion – Dafeng Rice Shop Paid 22 Yuan – Learned of the Scam by Calling the Public Works Bureau

Lou Yunyan, a 41-year-old man from Shaoxing, works as a carpenter. Recently, having been unemployed for a long time, he came up with a whimsical idea: he secretly printed a Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau inspector's permit at a printing shop, pasted his own photo on it, and stamped it with a forged seal of the Municipal Public Works Bureau. He specialized in extorting money in areas south, north, and west of Shanghai. There have been dozens of victims of his deception. The day before yesterday, Lou went to No. 70 Robert Road, West Shanghai, to the Dafeng Rice Shop opened by a Mr. Du from Wuxi. He claimed that the shop's awning was built without a permit and demanded a "materials fee" of 50 yuan in national currency. Mr. Du, seeing the permit, believed him and paid 22 yuan in national currency upfront, with the remainder to be collected the next day. After Lou left, Mr. Du called the Public Works Bureau and found out he had been scammed. He reported the incident to the Robert Road Police Station. Yesterday afternoon, Lou suddenly arrived in a rickshaw and demanded the remaining 28 yuan. Mr. Du immediately apprehended him and sent him to the police station, which then transferred him to the Caojiadu Public Security Sub-bureau for questioning. Lou confessed without denial. The sub-bureau, considering the case involved forgery of documents and impersonation of a public official, prepared a report to be sent to the General Bureau for strict handling.

Hong Qian Returns to China – To Become a Professor at Zhongda University

Hong Qian, a native of Sanyangchuan, She County, Huizhou, courtesy name Shoushi, is a top student of Liang Rengong. In 1939, he went to Germany and entered the University of Berlin to study philosophy. He then entered the University of Vienna in Austria and graduated in 1932, earning a doctorate. He then taught at the university for two years. When Zhong Wei Zou Lu went to Germany to attend the World University Presidents Conference, he hired Hong as his secretary and concurrently as a professor in the Department of Philosophy at Zhongshan University in Guangdong. Hong has now returned to China via the Siberian Railway and has arrived in Peiping. He has been lecturing at Peking University and Tsinghua University for several days, and has been warmly welcomed by the educational community in Peiping. It is said that he will go to Guangdong to take office in the near future. Hong has written many works in Austria, all of which are on logic, ethics, and natural philosophy. He plans to organize and print them after going to Guangdong.

Apuping Comes into Being

Apples made into powder, which is very effective in treating diarrhea, has long been proven and adopted by famous doctors in Europe. However, foreign goods are expensive and difficult to popularize. Jiufu Pharmaceutical Company on Baker Road, in view of this, carefully researched and used Yantai top-quality apples, finely crushed by machine, extracted all the effective ingredients, and made into powder with a specially made low-temperature dryer, refined and pressed into cakes, which is very effective in treating acute and chronic diarrhea in adults, and indigestion in children.

The center of the second hurricane was located within approximately 120 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 137 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM and is moving west-northwestward. Tilden and Vines Decide to Come to Shanghai for a Second Performance - Returning from the Philippines on the 20th of This Month for Another Performance - Order Arranged, Welcome Amateur Players to Participate in Guidance

The two world professional tennis giants, Tilden and Vines, passed through Shanghai the day before yesterday for a performance. Yesterday morning at 6:45, they took the original steamship, President Lincoln, south to Hong Kong, where they will have a performance competition, and then go to the Philippines for a performance. After finishing, they will take the original steamship back to the United States by the same route. It is expected that they will pass through Shanghai on the 20th of this month. The Pudda Trading Company in this city, which hosted the performance competition the day before yesterday, has already contacted the two and agreed that they will give another performance when they pass through Shanghai on the 20th, before returning to the United States.

Second Performance Order

After the performance the day before yesterday, Mr. Pymann, the manager of the Pudda Trading Company, immediately discussed the conditions for the second performance with Tilden at the International Hotel. The two parties fully agreed on the conditions, but the details are unknown. However, the general order of the performance has been roughly agreed upon. After Tilden and Vines have several performances with the Philippine professional tennis player Aragon in the Philippines, they will return to Shanghai by the same route. The order of the competition in Shanghai is expected to be two singles matches and one doubles match. Tilden will give a five-set singles performance match, and Vines will play a one-set singles match against Shanghai's best player, McGrath, and then Tilden and Vines will play doubles against Shanghai's one McGrath, or Cannavaro and one McGrath.

Welcome to Participate in Guidance Match

As for the "guidance" performance, amateur players of the first class in Shanghai are welcome to participate in this "guidance" performance. However, the consent of the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association must be obtained first. Yamagishi, the Japanese Davis Cup player, had this so-called "guidance" performance against Vines in Japan this time. The ticket prices for the second performance on November 20 have been set at three types: five yuan, three yuan, and two yuan.

Tilden's Retirement Issue

Before Tilden and Vines left Shanghai, they were asked when Tilden would retire from his tennis career. Tilden replied that he suffered a slight injury to his arm during a performance in the United States this spring, and it has not yet fully recovered, but it is gradually improving. As for when he will retire, if he can still give a good performance to the audience, and the audience feels it is worth paying to watch, he will not retire. When he finds that he is regressing, he will retire immediately.

Beijing-Shanghai Tennis Match Concludes - Beijing Champion Ma Shaobo Loses to Cai Huiquan - Beijing Team Completely Defeated - Shanghai Wins 7-0

The Beijing-Shanghai tennis competition was held yesterday morning and afternoon at the China Association court on Singapore Road. The strength of both sides was considerable, but as a result, the China Association took advantage of its home advantage and won a complete victory of seven to zero. In the performance matches, it won two and drew one. The Silver Ball Sword, a gift from the Director of the Beijing Social Bureau, was presented by Mrs. Zhao Henghai as a prize, and was accepted by Chen Qihao, the leader of the Chinese team. He hoped that the Beijing-Shanghai tennis friendship match could be held once a year in the spring and autumn seasons, so that they could learn from each other's mistakes and achieve unity. The battle situation is recorded below.

Cai-Ma Battle - Among yesterday's group matches, the first singles match between Ma Shaobo and Cai Huiquan was the most noticed. Ma has recently become a champion in the capital and is indeed a rising star in Beijing. Cai recently participated in Wimbledon and returned. Yesterday's battle was quite exciting. Ma's hitting style is very stable and his strokes are powerful, but there is too little variation. Cai's hitting style is very good and his strategy is also correct. It is a pity that he does not have enough physical strength, otherwise he would be a formidable figure. In terms of strength, he should be above Ma. In the first set, Cai made many mistakes, and Ma won easily with a score of 6-1. However, from the second set onwards, Cai gradually improved. Although Ma took the lead with a score of 4-3, Cai won three consecutive games with extremely beautiful diagonal shots, taking back one set with a score of 6-4. In the third set, Cai became more and more brave and continued his long and short shots from left and right, taking the lead with scores of 3-1 and 5-2. At this time, Ma was exhausted from running and showed panic, and announced his surrender. The score was 6-3. The overall results are as follows.

Yesterday's Western League A Group Football - Jinan Loses to Luxe - 5-1, 2-1 at Halftime

The Jinan football team met Luxe yesterday at Shenyuan for the Western League A Group match. Luxe is one of the top four teams this season, and the outcome was already expected. However, Jinan played hard yesterday, and Luxe did not look very energetic, so the match ended with a score of 9-1. Luxe won, with a score of 2-1 at halftime. The audience was very small, about 300 people. The lineups are as follows:

First Half - Luxe attacked first. Within eight minutes, both sides had shots that hit the post. Jinan launched a major counterattack, but failed to score. Soon after, Jinan encountered two more dangerous situations, both of which were saved by Ye Peichu. The Luxe army took advantage of the situation to attack, reaching the gate. Gelinbo flew and shot low, entering from the left corner. Luxe took the lead with a score of 2-1. At this time, about three minutes before the break, Jinan's offensive turned strong. Chen Nianjin hooked from the baseline, swept through the ball fight, and Eckhoff missed his foot. No one was in front of the goal, and Zeng Rongzhong was too late to catch up. The shot was caught. At this time, the ball was not far out and turned to the right. Liu Shizan hooked back to the center line, and Wu Shufen shot fiercely at the penalty line. The shoe and the ball flew together, cutting into the net and breaking the duck egg record, making the score 2-1. Two minutes later, the first half ended.

Second Half - The battle started again. Three minutes into the half, the Luxe army launched a fierce attack. Adige hooked from the baseline, and the ball fell beside the left post of the goal, less than a foot away. Yan Lianjin and Bolingai competed for the ball, hooking and picking with their knees. Unexpectedly, Yan turned cleverness into clumsiness and sent a gift, making the score 3-1. Jinan lost many good opportunities and has since been depressed. After 20 minutes, neither side had made any achievements. After a long time, Qinxun, a veteran of Luxe, got a chance at the door and opened the record again. Not even a minute later, Lei Ying got a pass from Kokelan and headed the ball into the net, making the score 5-1. Because of Luxe's excessive bravery, Gelinbo and Keke Leng were successively injured and left the field. Soon after, the game ended, and Jinan lost 5-1.

The Reflections We Should Have After the World Games

— Shao Rugan

The Eleventh World Games, which attracted worldwide attention, have been over for a long time. Recalling the German preparations’ comprehensiveness, the venue layout's novelty, the audience’s enthusiasm, the order’s excellence, and the breakthrough of various sports records at the Games, this great historical achievement is so worthy of praise and commemoration. Military songs and cheers echoed, the flags of the meeting and national flags waved together, and hundreds of thousands of people gathered, showing the popularity of various races. The unprecedented grand occasion was deeply imprinted in the minds of the audience, and no one can forget it, only recall it with longing, remember it forever, and think of it forever. Since Hitler took office in Germany, it has been known as the Third Reich. National rejuvenation and national strength are praised by everyone. This conference was held in Berlin. All kinds of construction and organizations all showed the spirit of a dazzling new country, burying themselves in hard work, and painstakingly researching, which is really admirable. The construction of various parts of the venue required more than 30 million. Fifty-two countries participated. There were more than 5,000 male and female athletes, and more than 100,000 people attended the sports performances and youth training personnel from various countries. The Games had 1,200 referees, 1,200 assistant referees, 400 office staff, and more than 12,000 others assisting with the Games' affairs, such as transportation and telecommunications.

This conference not only displayed the spirit of sports competitions to observe the sports technology achievements of athletes from various countries, but also had sports performances from various countries and grand gatherings, such as sports exhibitions and art and science exhibitions, one to display the spirit of the World Games, and one to display the spirit of German revival. The leisure and entertainment discussion held in Hamburg, the international sports camp in Aus, and the large group callisthenics performance of thousands of male and female children and young people, the entire conference, in addition to paying attention to sports competitions, can also take into account the discussion and lectures on sports theory. This is something that previous World Games have not been able to do. The bell of the Berlin Olympics welcomed athletes from various countries back to their motherland, and the technology and spirit of the conference will continue to be promoted. The meeting song and meeting emblem will be kept forever. In 1940, this kind of human race sports performance will be held in Tokyo, Japan. Learning from the past and planning for the future, how should we hone and strive to make full preparations?

Our country participated in the World Games this time, with a delegation of 141 people. The grand organization, European figures and the people of Berlin paid great attention to our sports. The athletes' representatives participated in various sports and did their best. However, their physique was inferior to others, and their energy was inferior to others, so that the sports competition lagged behind in every aspect and failed everywhere. In the international martial arts arena, we could not hold our heads high and raise our eyebrows. The flagpoles on the scoreboard could not display our national flag. Now, let's not complain about fate, but blame the weakness of the Chinese race.

In the cold wind and bitter rain, our delegation left Berlin and returned to Shanghai on October 3rd. As defeated generals and a humiliating army, we were ridiculed and mocked. What else can we say? How can we bear to say it? It is often said that it is easy to be an athlete's representative, but it is difficult to be an athlete's representative of a country that has no international achievements. Victory is gratifying, but defeat is difficult to show to others. These words are not only for the athletes who attended the World Games in our country this time. Perhaps what the athletes want to say in their hearts is, alas, their ambitions have not been realized, and their hearts are depressed. Where else can they complain?

However, the fact of failure is after all before our eyes. Sarcasm and sneers are good lessons after failure. We must find a way to win in failure in order to wash away the shame of failure.

Over the long years, the delegation has returned to China for more than a month. How to strive for progress, I think the sports authorities are designing and preparing. Now, let's first put forward the important issues after the World Games for discussion.

(1) There Must Be a Sound Sports Administrative Organization

The sports administrative organization is the backbone of all sports undertakings. Tracing its evolutionary process, it mostly tends to political organization. Use the government's greatest determination and the power of politics to determine a precise and sound sports administrative organization as a driving force. Concentrate thinking, unify steps, and let the government allocate annual business expenses and work hard, then the sports undertakings of our Chinese nation may have hope of progress. At present, the highest sports administrative organizations in our country are the Sports Department and the National Sports Committee of the Ministry of Education, which handle national school sports, social sports, and scout and military training affairs. The Central Civil Training Department has a Sports Guidance Section and the National Sports Planning Committee, which handle the sports guidance affairs of party departments and mass organizations at all levels. The Training Headquarters also has a Sports Section to pay attention to the promotion of military sports undertakings. Different paths lead to the same goal, guiding and developing their respective sports undertakings. However, the administrative organization is slightly different. In fact, in promoting undertakings, it is inevitable that there will be a situation of duplication of efforts. There are few opportunities for communication, which loses the power of lotus connection and progress. We must refer to the trends of sports administration in various countries and adapt to the urgent needs of our Chinese nation to build a sports administrative organization of the era. On the 7th of last month, the first National Sports Design Committee meeting of the Central Civil Training Department had a suggestion on the central sports administrative group to concentrate and merge the above three parts and organize it under the control of the national supreme leader. The general idea of this case is to hand it over for review. If it can be realized, then the matters of sports should be promoted and reformed in our country will definitely be effective. Under the supervision and guidance of the central government, complete the provincial and municipal sports administrative groups in the shortest possible time, then all promotion undertakings will easily achieve the effect of pointing arms.

(2) School Sports

After the content of sports courses in schools at all levels and the key points of homework for each academic year are promulgated by the Ministry of Education, there are many who comply with and strictly implement them, but there are also those who perfunctorily follow the old ways. In terms of universities, it is not appropriate to give up and let them be free. We should strictly popularize sports. For freshmen and sophomores, at least two hours of sports per week should be required courses. High school and junior high school should follow the ministry's orders. Military training and scout training time should not encroach on the original sports time. Extracurricular activities and outdoor life should be actively promoted. The content of elementary school sports courses needs to be improved. The key points of homework for each academic year should be detailed, and sports standards must be formulated to cultivate the virtues of hard work, endurance, courage, obedience, liveliness, and happiness. Standard tests should be tried out. Those who cannot meet the standards should not be promoted or graduated. In addition, youth training and youth labor service should also be vigorously promoted as the basis for protecting the country and strengthening the race.

(3) Social Sports

Europeans and Americans have developed sports habits, and their interest in sports is strong. Children, young people, and all walks of life in society have sports habits, and talents emerge in large numbers. There is a reason for this. In our country, sports seem to be occupied by school students. The public rarely consults them. Therefore, social sports are also the most difficult thing to do effectively. How to create a strong sports atmosphere is the first problem to promote mass sports. Sports practitioners must go deep into the people, approach the people, and welcome the people to the venue to exercise. At the same time, they should investigate the local material environment, distribute and set up small-scale sports venues, hold sports competitions, and sports performances. Regarding folk sports, they should also be promoted more so that the sports venue becomes a center for promoting sports undertakings and a central agency for the implementation of mass education, so that the public recognizes the important significance of sports and gradually develops their love of sports. I think that the mass sports undertakings that are completely unpredictable will eventually reach the day we seek. Dear compatriots, our physique is not enough to compete with Europeans and Americans. At the Asian Games in Tokyo in the future, can our Chinese nation hold its head high and breathe easily? It all depends on preparing early and preparing quickly. (End)

The Municipal No. 1 Sports Field: Chess Competition Held

Due to the needs of those who come to the Municipal No. 1 Sports Field for exercise, a chess competition will be held. The competition will be held every evening. Registration will start on the 9th of this month and end on the 23rd. The origin of the competition is recorded as follows:

The field previously thought that athletes should have proper entertainment during rest to adjust themselves. Otherwise, people living together without anything to do easily talk about things that are not righteous. Therefore, chess was specially set up for leisure after exercise.

A chess game requires a calm attitude, meticulous thinking, and perseverance. These qualities are complementary and not contradictory to the edification of various sports. Therefore, it is quite popular among athletes.

Over the years, the number of people who love it has increased, and the interest has become stronger. Recently, more people have requested to hold a competition to achieve the effect of observation and mutual learning. This is the reason for the birth of this chess competition. The competition time is after 7:00 pm every evening, which does not hinder the work, practice, and sports of all walks of life. The main point is to use the spirit of the New Life Movement to eliminate the bad habits of chess playing in the past. It is also hoped that it will be recognized by those who know.

Textile Goods: Native Cotton Cloth Factory Market Prices Repeatedly Increase

Although the overseas cotton market has continuously declined and the exchange's yarn prices have repeatedly fallen, the price of native cotton cloth has increased because Japanese trading companies have raised prices for fine cloth, No. 84 cloth, and market cloth for December delivery by five cents per bolt again today. Over the past few days, the total increase has been ten to twenty cents per bolt, leading to increased buying interest in the market. Because of the continuous downward trend in the market in recent days, factories and traders have generally adopted a wait-and-see attitude. Now, they are rushing to replenish their stocks, and demand is high, so the market has turned around. Therefore, although yarn and cotton prices fell today, cloth prices continue to rise. Fine cloth, suitable for dyeing blue, is in urgent demand due to the current season. The base price of No. 84 cloth and market cloth is still low, and demand is expected to increase gradually in the future. Therefore, the price increase has exceeded ten to fifteen cents per bolt. The base price of fine twill is already high, and it has also increased by five cents per bolt. However, sales of coarse cloth, coarse twill, and colored cloth, straight tribute cloth, serge, woolen cloth, flannel, and white flannel remain sluggish, and a turnaround is unlikely. Transactions are mainly with local stores and traders. Sales to some customers from Tianjin, Changsha, Hankou, and Guangzhou in the north and south are slightly better, but most customers are still reluctant to purchase new, expensive goods because cheap goods are still difficult to sell locally.

Long-haired Camel Down Still Popular: Used by the Bourgeoisie, Sixty Yuan Is Not Expensive

The new silk-woven long-haired camel down that was popular the year before last is still popular now. Generally, the upper class or bourgeoisie choose this material for men's and women's overcoats. A typical long-haired camel down overcoat costs an average of over sixty yuan in national currency, and a slightly better one costs no less than one hundred yuan, because the wholesale market price is more than ten yuan per yard, and higher quality ones are more than twenty yuan. Fabric stores all have orders. N绒 numbers on Qipan Street do not sell it, but Ruishiwen, Shili Luo and other foreign companies all have stock and sales are very active.

Children's Special

Toys

— Yiyiguan Lord

I recently saw the Tianjin telegraph news published in this newspaper saying: "According to a customs survey, from January to September of this year, the total value of Japanese toys imported into North China was 5 million yuan, an increase of 35% compared to last year."

After reading the above telegraph news, I feel that "toys" are originally the gift of children. It can also be said that all children love "toys." This is not only true for the children in our country, but also for the children in your noble country. Then, we welcome other people's "toys," as long as we have "toys," other people will also come to welcome them. What is so rare about the mere "5 million yuan"?

However, what is terrible is that other people's "toys" can deceive our money. And our "toys" cannot only deceive other people's money. On the contrary, they are used by others as a kind of aggressive "toy"!

Alas! Someone asked me: What kind of "toy" is this? Is it a dog? Is it a pig? I said: This is a kind of "toy" that is similar to that, that is, those "traitors" and puppets!

Casual Talks About Children's Anecdotes

— Yisheng

Xiao Wu Changed Crying

When Emperor Jianwen collapsed, Emperor Xiaowu ascended the throne. At that time, he was only a little over ten years old. According to the imperial rules, when the old emperor died and a new emperor took over, the young emperor had to go to the spirit tablet every evening to cry, which was called "crying." However, Emperor Xiaowu did not go to cry very often. The people around him thought that he was too young to understand the rules, so they explained it to him and asked him to abide by the rules and go to cry every day. Emperor Xiaowu said: "I will naturally cry when I feel sad. How can I force myself to do this crying thing every day?" He still "went his own way" and only went to the spirit tablet when he really wanted to cry, and did not hold a crying ceremony on time.

Etiquette was originally created based on human sentiment. However, worldly etiquette is practiced too rigidly and becomes hypocritical, which is even more comical! But look at the funeral ceremonies held in ordinary people's homes now: when the mourner walks to the spirit tablet, the master of ceremonies shouts loudly, and the crying sound in the filial mourning immediately follows, a loud wailing and unrestrained excitement, called holding a funeral; when the master of ceremonies finishes shouting, the crying sound will also quickly disappear. Such a cycle of ups and downs forms a law, can't the master of ceremonies be called the "crying commander"? There are many other ridiculous etiquettes that are too numerous to mention. They should be reformed according to the situation, and there is no need to adhere to them rigidly. Xiaowu criticized that corrupt etiquette and resolutely went his own way, which was purely out of the innocence of a child; in that medieval era of worshiping etiquette, being in the imperial position as a model for subjects, this kind of behavior was not easy to obtain! Today, people do not need to be rigid and against their feelings about etiquette, nor do they need to overcorrect or even completely abolish them. They only need to recognize the rationale and act accordingly.

Manure

— Dong Xun

"Ten Thousand Taels of Gold" someone calls it that! Although manure is a stinky thing that makes people fearful, it can be used as fertilizer to help rice seedlings grow out of golden rice, which is evidence of its contribution to people!

The food we send into our mouths is first secreted by saliva in the oral cavity to turn starch into soluble sugar: gastric juice is secreted in the stomach to digest protein; the bile and pancreatic juice remaining in the intestine can also digest fat, and the digested food is then sent to the cells in all parts of the body through the intestinal membrane and blood vessels, but the substances that cannot be absorbed in the intestine become manure! It is excreted from the excretory cavity!

Speaking of manure, it also has many ingredients:

(1) Undigested food residue (such as fat, protein, and carbohydrates)

(2) Indigestible substances (such as fiber, chlorophyll, etc.)

(3) Difficult-to-digest substances (such as raw starch, pity acid salts, etc.)

(4) Various bacteria and dead cells of the intestinal mucosa

(5) Bile residue

From manure, we can create many plant-based foods, which is the so-called "taking from people" and then "using it for people," and the cycle continues!

Children, don't underestimate manure! Although it is a stinky thing!

Spinning Girl

— Da Zhai

Spinning Girl,

Wailing and crying;

The sound of spinning all night,

Both lifelike and wonderful;

Seemingly sympathizing with Gandhi's non-cooperation,

Calling for the restoration of national economic freedom;

The spinning wheel is his constant companion,

Spinning the wheel is his daily work;

A cry to promote domestic goods,

This singing and that harmony is really lively;

Until late autumn,

Early autumn leaves and west wind;

They all disappear without a trace,

But there is not a single strand or thread to be used as cold clothes;

When things come to a head,

I can't save myself even if I want to save myself,

The root of this disease is that I can only talk but can't act,

Only caring about singing empty slogans;

Don't sing empty slogans!

Don't sing empty slogans!

It is better to do everything down-to-earth.

Small Discussion

— Yongren

It was getting dark.

Zhi'er and De'er were sitting in the courtyard, telling stories to pass the time. Suddenly, a bat flew very low and passed over De'er's head. This swoop seemed to start De'er's doubts: he immediately asked Zhi'er:

"Brother! Some people say that this bat is a bird, and some people say that it is a beast. Which category do you think it belongs to?"

"Guess what! What exactly is it?" Zhi'er asked De'er back with a smile.

"I said that the bat is a bird," De'er said firmly.

"Why?"

"It has wings to fly, isn't that proof that it is a bird?"

"Well, you are wrong! What it uses to fly is not wings. It's just that its front toes are very long, and the skin is stretched between the toes to connect them, so it looks like wings.

The bat does not have the sharp beak of a bird, but the lips and teeth of a beast; what covers its body is not feathers but fur; it has very long ears; and it does not lay eggs, so at first glance, the shape of the bat seems to be a bird, but in fact it is a beast!"

Do you believe that there is carbon in sugar?

— Yongyan

The sweet white sugar that we eat every day actually contains a lot of carbon. This sentence seems a bit bizarre on the surface, but it is absolutely true and does not deceive people: sugar does contain carbon, and if you don't believe it, we can find a way to take out the carbon inside.

We can take a teaspoon of white sugar for seasoning from the kitchen and put it on the lid of a cigarette can or another tin can: then clamp the lid with iron tongs and put it on the flame of an alcohol lamp or a coal stove and heat it vigorously. When burning, the white sugar gradually melts and turns into a brown liquid, and finally it burns into a black solid. This black thing does not taste like anything on the tongue, and it will burn by itself when put in a fire; what is this thing? It is the "carbon" we mentioned above.

Facts are the most eloquent. After doing the above small experiment, we extracted black carbon from the sweet sugar with our own hands; we can rest assured that sugar does contain carbon, but the carbon in the sugar has changed its appearance, so we don't recognize it.

Now you can write this down in your notebook.

Karma

— Huren

A fox ran panting, followed by a hunting dog and a hunter, who were also following closely behind. Although the fox ran extremely fast, the hunting dog refused to let it go.

The fox ran for a long time and met a woodcutter who was carrying a load of firewood from across the street. "Uncle! Please...save...me! Behind...the hunting dog...is chasing after me!" It begged with a very pitiful expression. "No, you stole two of my chicks the day before yesterday. You hateful thing, now you are asking me?" After saying that, he left without looking back. The fox went on its way very disappointedly.

The fox ran for a long time again and saw a sheep mother sewing clothes in front of the house, so it begged piteously again, "Grandma sheep! Please be compassionate and let me...hide in your house...The hunter is chasing behind!" "Bah! You bad kind! You're here again! You stole one of my sons the night before yesterday, and you're here again today?" She rushed over in anger as if fire was coming out of her eyes. The fox had to turn around and escape again.

After two rests, the distance between the fox and the hunting dog became closer.

It saw a tabby cat sleeping on the ground, "Miss Cat, please...hurry...save me!...The hunter is coming...!" "Hush! No! You are the worst thing in our village, go, go quickly!"

"Bang!" With a sound, the fox fell in response, and the hunting dog rushed up and bit it in one bite.

Backbone

— Zhaifu

The two words "backbone" represent a person's style. We praise those with strong wills and noble character as having "backbone," while those with weak wills and base character are said to "lack backbone." Throughout history, loyal ministers, righteous warriors, and steadfast martyrs have all been people with backbone; the ungrateful and those who sell their country for personal gain are people without backbone. Flesh and skin are soft, but if a person has no bones, they are just a mass of flesh and skin, unable to stand upright or move! If bones are not strong and solid, how can one bear heavy burdens and travel far?

During the Ming Dynasty, Yang Jiaoshan, a loyal minister who was framed and killed by the treacherous minister Yan Song, had a couplet: "Iron shoulders bear the burden of righteousness, a sharp hand composes articles." The so-called "iron shoulders" and "sharp hand" refer to the backbone of loyal and righteous individuals.

Throughout history, the downfall of many countries has not been at the hands of enemies, but at the hands of traitors who lacked backbone and willingly became the running dogs of the enemy.

Why would a good citizen become a traitor? Is it because they lack clothing or food? Individuals like Yin Rugeng were originally officials in the service of their own government, enjoying a life of luxury; they were not driven by hunger or cold! It was simply because they were never nurtured with the backbone to be a proper human being.

"Strong grass is known in a strong wind; a loyal minister is known in chaotic times." Those with backbone, the more difficult their circumstances and the more chaotic the world, the more they must demonstrate their integrity in serving the country loyally.

To become a loyal and righteous person in the future, one must cultivate the backbone of loyalty and righteousness from childhood; to cultivate the backbone of loyalty and righteousness, one must possess the following tenets for establishing oneself:

Do not covet luxury!

Do not entertain extravagant fantasies!

Do not yield to violence!

Do not bully the weak and the poor!

Do not love money!

Do not fear death!

Little Black Charcoal

(1) A child sees a chair with a broken leg.

(2) The leg is fixed, making it look like a complete chair.

(3) Little Black Charcoal walks along reading a book, sees a chair, and sits down.

(4) Haha! Little Black Charcoal falls over!

Speech Practice

— Zhuying

For anyone who wants to convey their meaning and gain understanding and sympathy from others, an engaging speech is indispensable. In the election contests of politicians, the most effective weapon is speech, used to announce one's aspirations and policies, creating a good impression on the audience and inspiring them to cast their votes with sympathy. This is true for politicians, and it's also true for academics. An academic with in-depth research, on the one hand, can publish their research findings in writing, but at the same time, they must also have excellent speaking skills to be used when invited by schools or organizations to give speeches. Even an entrepreneur who has created excellent products needs excellent speech to assist in promotion. In short, regardless of what field one will serve in the future, every child should strive to practice speech.

The most difficult step in practicing speech is being able to speak on stage as if no one else is there. Generally, those who practice speech always have a good idea in their mind and make ample preparations before going on stage. But when they step onto the stage and see dozens or hundreds of eyes staring directly at their face, they suddenly blush, their heart pounds violently, and their mouth seems sealed, unable to open. The more anxious they become, the less they can say. Even if they force out a few sentences, it is difficult for the audience to understand. This is a common ailment among those who are new to speech. But this shyness is not difficult to eradicate. If the first time on stage is a failure, don't be discouraged; gather your courage and go on stage again the second time. Continue with persistent effort the third and fourth times. At most, it will not exceed the tenth time, and you will surely develop a thick skin that will absolutely not blush, and a calm heart that will absolutely not pound violently when you step on the stage. By then, even when standing in front of dozens or hundreds of eyes, you will be able to calmly and casually articulate what you want to say, one by one, from your mouth.

The material for a speech, regardless of its quality, must be organized like an essay, so that listeners can understand everything in an organized manner and feel clear and comprehensible. If you can also insert some interesting stories or anecdotes in each section to prevent listeners from feeling bored, that would naturally be even better. Therefore, it is best to extract a few main points of the speech in advance, so that there will be no mistakes when speaking. The posture during the speech should be as dignified and natural as possible, absolutely avoiding any forced or artificial attitude. The voice should not be too high or too low, because if it is too low, the audience will not be able to hear clearly, and if it is too high, it will not produce harmonious and pleasing sounds in the audience's eardrums. The most appropriate volume is only half a notch louder than ordinary conversation, which is enough. When speaking, slightly raising your head can also help to expand the sound waves.

Children, do you also want to become a speaker in the future? Speech is not a difficult thing. If you are happy, you can hold speech practice sessions once or twice every week in your class. After a year or two, you will already have a lot of experience.

Where Does Silk Come From?

— Yang Zhigang

The clothes we wear are made of cotton, silk, or other materials. I think the clothes children like the most must be those made of silk! However, many children do not know the origin of silk. Now I will tell you:

First, take the silkworm eggs (Figure 1) and incubate them. In a few days, many small silkworms will hatch (Figure 2). After the small silkworms hatch, immediately gather mulberry leaves (Figure 3). The mulberry leaves that are gathered are too big for the small silkworms to eat, so they must be cut into small pieces (Figure 4). Feed the cut mulberry leaves to the small silkworms (Figure 5). After a few days, the small silkworms will start to sleep! After many days, they will sleep four times in a row (Figure 6). After the fourth sleep, they will go onto the frame and start to spin cocoons (Figure 7). Take the cocoons down and reel the silk (Figure 8). Use machines to weave the reeled silk into silk fabrics (Figure 9).

Our country produces a lot of silk fabrics, especially Zhejiang and other provinces. A large amount is exported to foreign countries every year (Figure 10).

However, the price of silk has plummeted recently. The reasons for this are the abundance of rayon in the market and the poor quality of silk production. As a result, it cannot be widely sold domestically and cannot be promoted abroad. Looking back at our neighbor Japan, their silkworm farming methods were originally learned from us, but because they study and know how to improve, their results are very good. We must work hard to study and improve!

Filial Piety (3)

— Hai

However, Perskov trusted in the kindness of Heaven. Now that it had given her that precious passport, it would certainly help her overcome all other difficulties. She trusted Heaven on the one hand, and on the other hand, she was full of self-confidence, believing that as long as she was determined, no resistance would be a problem. Finally, she got her parents' permission and was scheduled to leave on September 8th.

That morning, as soon as it dawned, she was already dressed and ready, with a small leather bag slung over her shoulder. Her father wanted her to take the only silver ruble in the house, but she refused to accept it, saying that the money was really not enough to cover her travel expenses to Petersburg, and it was better to leave it at home, as it might be needed. But her father sternly ordered her to take it, and she had no choice but to accept it. Two poor neighbors also insisted on giving her all the money they had, a total of thirty copper kopecks and a twenty-kopeck silver coin, but she resolutely refused. She only thanked them for their kindness and sincerely promised them that she would do her best to help them, as they might have the hope of being pardoned as well.

When the first ray of sunlight shone into the room, it illuminated a brief moment of solemn silence, according to the beautiful ancient Russian custom, to bless the traveler with a safe journey. Then they said a few more words to each other, gave one last embrace, Perskov knelt down to receive her parents' blessing, then stood up and resolutely set out—a nineteen-year-old girl, with only one silver ruble in her pocket, walking through vast forests, traveling far to Petersburg to see the dignified emperor.

The two poor neighbors, to show their kindness, especially accompanied her out of Iji Village, until they met a group of girls who happened to be going the same way to a small village, and entrusted them to take good care of her, then told her to take care. On the way, they were disturbed for a while by a few half-drunk young men and suffered some minor scares, but they finally drove them away. When they arrived at the small village, Perskov spent the night there peacefully. The next morning, she felt very tired, but after setting out, she couldn't help but be a little afraid of the loneliness on the road. However, when she thought of the blessing of the angels, her courage immediately returned; but because she was not familiar with the road, she walked for a long time in vain and still returned to the village where she had spent the night. She continued to go forward with great hardship, and still could not avoid getting lost often. Every time she asked people for the way to Petersburg, everyone always laughed at her. She didn't even know the name of the nearest place. All she knew was that she had to pass through Kyiv, a place called the holy town by the Russians. So every time people said they didn't know the way to Petersburg, she busily asked how to get to Kyiv. One day, she came to a fork in the road and saw several travelers passing by in a carriage, so she hurried to ask which road led to Kyiv. They laughed and replied, "You can walk any road you like, it's all good. These three roads can take you to Kyiv, Paris, or Rome." She had no choice but to choose the middle road to go, and fortunately she did not go wrong. However, she could not figure out any of the villages she passed along the way. Every time she came to a small village and asked for lodging in a humble house, she often received better treatment, but once she arrived in a big place, people regarded her as a suspicious woman and refused to take her in.
